2a1(zha): gcig na/ de bzhin gshegs pa yang dag par rdzogs
2a2(zha): pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das longs spyod chen po/ phyogs bcu dus
2a3(zha): bzhi'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo
2a4(zha): rje'i bdag nyid ma lus mi lus lus pa med pa thams cad dang so so ma yin/ tha
2b1(zha): mi dang / dbyer med pa'i rang bzhin te/ 'og min gyi gnas mtha' dang dbus med pa na/ gzhi tshad med
2b2(zha): pa'i ye shes kyi 'khor lo gsal ba la/ ye shes rin po che sna tshogs 'bar ba'i gzhal yas khang rgya
2b3(zha): phyogs bcur yongs su ma chad pa/ yon tan dpag tu med par rgyas pa'i phyir gru bzhir gyur pa/ lhag
2b4(zha): pa'i ye shes rin po che'i blo 'bur gyis mdzes pa/ rtse mo phyogs bcu dus bzhi'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing dkyil
2b5(zha): 'khor ma lus pa thams cad so so ma yin/ ngo bo nyid gcig pa'i ye shes kun tu 'khyil pa/ ye shes
3a1(zha): @##/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ ye shes rin po che'i dbyibs dang kha dog la sogs pa rnam pa tha dad pa'i bye brag
3a2(zha): dang khyad par du gyur pa/ dpags pa/ tshad dpag tu med pa/ ye shes rin po che 'phreng ba dang / chun 'phyang dang / shar
3a3(zha): bu'i rgyan dang / gzugs sna tshogs dang / sgra sna tshogs dang / dri sna tshogs dang / ro sna tshogs dang / reg bya sna tshogs kyis/
3a4(zha): phyogs bcur 'khrig par rang byung la/ mi sgrib par gsal ba'i rgyan bsam gyis mi khyab par klubs pa/ rnam par thar pa bzhi'i
3a5(zha): sgo nas 'jug pa'i sgo khyud can/ rnam par thar pa brgyad kyi rta babs dang ldan pa/ phyi nang med pa/ kun tu yang nang du gyur pa na/ mi
3a6(zha): 'jigs pa'i seng ge'i khri dang / stobs kyi glang po che'i khri dang / rdzu 'phrul rta'i khri dang / dbang gi rma bya'i khri dang / thogs pa med
3b1(zha): pa nam mkha' lding gi khri dang / rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba nyi zla'i dkyil 'khor dang / gos pa med pa'i pad+ma rin po che'i gdan la/ sku mdun dang rgyab med pa
3b2(zha): thams cad du zhal thal le bar gsal zhing mtshan dang dpe byad du ldan pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa thams cad du/ skra gsung thugs sna tshogs par kun tu snang ba/
3b3(zha): lhan gyis grub pa'i sku gsung thugs chen po las/ thabs dang shes rab kyi zhabs gnyis mnyam pa'i brtul zhugs kyi skyil mo krung du bzhugs pa/ ye shes drug
3b4(zha): gi phyag rgya/ ye shes chen po'i phyag rgya 'bar ba can/ sku gsung thugs bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dbu gsum dang ldan pa/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam
3b5(zha): bar shes pa'i rgyal po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gzugs kyi rgyal po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa tshor ba'i rgyal po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa 'du shes kyi rgyal po dang /
3b6(zha): de bzhin gshegs pa 'du byed kyi rgyal po dang / de dag kun kyang mthing kha dang / dkar po dang / sar po dang / le brgan dang / ljang khu'i mdog tu 'tsher ba/ btsun
3b7(zha): mo dam pa snang ba'i dbyings dang / sra ba'i dbyings dang / mnyem pa'i dbyings dang / dro ba'i dbyings dang / bskyod pa'i dbyings la sogs pa/ btsun mo'i tshogs
4a1(zha): dang gnyis su med par chos kyi dbyings kun tu mtha' yas par khyab pa ni/ 'di lta ste/ dper na til gyi gang bu bzhin du gang nas khyab par bzhugs
4a2(zha): so// de nas byang chub chen po rdo rje mthong ba dang / byang chub chen po rdo rje thos pa dang / byang chub chen po rdo rje snom pa dang / byang chub chen po rdo rje myong ba dang /
4a3(zha): btsun mo mthong bar bya ba dang / mnyan par bya ba dang / snom par bya ba dang / myong bar bya ba'i tshogs dang / byang chub chen po rdo rje mthong byed dang / byang chub chen po rdo rje
4a4(zha): thos byed dang / byang chub chen po rdo rje snom byed dang / byang chub che rdo rje myong byed dang / btsun mo 'das pa dang / da ltar da / 'byung ba dang / ma byon pa'i tshogs dang /
4a5(zha): 'joms pa chen po reg pa dang / 'joms pa chen po reg byed dang / 'joms po chen po reg bya dang / 'joms pa chen po reg shes dang / btsun mo rtag par ma yin pa dang
4a6(zha): chad par ma yin pa dang / bdag tu ma yin pa dang / mtshan mar ma yin pa la sogs pa/ de lta bu'i tshogs brjod kyis mi lang ba dang gnyis su med par bzhugs so//
4a7(zha): de nas de bzhin gshegs pa btsun mo'i tshogs dang gnyis su med pa'i gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor de dag nyid kyi gsang ba 'di nyid/ sku dang / gsung dang /
4b1(zha): thugs dang / yon tan dang / 'phrin las rdo rje las phyung ngo // e a ma a ma'o// de bzhin nyid kyi dbyings nyid dbang sgyur ye shes dkyil 'khor thugs rje'i dang //
4b2(zha): rang snang ba nyid ting 'dzin gzugs brnyan sgyu ma rnam dag gsal ba ni// sku gsung thugs dang yon tan 'phrin las sel med pa yi yinate/ yid bzhin rin po che// mi zad par
4b3(zha): ldan rgyan gyi 'khor lo rdo rje mchog gi gnas nyid do// zhes rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig tu'o// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ gleng gzhi'i le'u ste dang po'o// /
4b4(zha): / de nas bcom ldan 'das byed pa po rdo rje yid kun tu bzang po thams cad ma lus pa'i rang bzhin gyi tshul rdo rje/ btsun mo bya ba mo chos kun tu bzang mo la 'jug
4b5(zha): par gyur te/ ched du brjod pa'i nga brjod do// oM/ chos kyi chos nyid shes bya'i dbyings// kun tu bzang mo bde ba'i yum// ma g.yos rang bzhin dkyil 'khor ni//
4b6(zha): bdag yin bdag gi spyod yul ba// phyag rgya sna tshogs so sor gsal// nub phyogs 'og min gnas mchog tu// ma chags pad+ma'i gdan bting ba// dus gsum /
4b7(zha): rgyal ba bzhugs pa'i gnas// rnam par thar pa'i sgo bzhi la// phyag rgya bzhi dang yang dag ldan// dbang dang skal med bsal ba'i phyir// nang gtan phyi rim lcags
5a1(zha): dang ldan// rgyal ba yongs kyis sbas pa yi// sus kyang gting dpag dka' ba de// kun tu bzang po nyid kyis gzigs// zhes brjod
5a2(zha): pas/ btsun mo byab mo chis kun tu bzang mo la 'jug par gyur to// zhugs nas btsun mo bya ba mo chos kun tu bzang mos/ bcom ldan 'das yi kun tu bzang po
5a3(zha): dang gnyis su med pa'i longs spyod pade ba la mnyam par gnas te/ ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// sems kyi sems nyid byed pa'i gtso// kun tu bzang po rdo rje'i
5a4(zha): yid// ye shes drug gi rang bzhin te// shar phyogs mngon dga'i bsam ya sa na// nI la lta bu'i gter 'byin pa// gsang 'dus 'phrul gyi lde mig gis// rnam
5a5(zha): par thar pa'i sgo phye nas// byang chub mchog gi nang gtan bkrol// mnyam sbor pad+ma'i gdan la bzhugs// 'gro don byang chub sems bskyed nas// 'gro lnga skye shi'i dbang

5a7(zha): bzhin gshegs pa ma lus pathams cad gcig gi rang bzhin du dbyer med pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa nyid de bzhin gshegs pa nyid la ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// e mdo
5b1(zha): rdo rje phung po'i yan lag ni// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas lnga ru grags// skye mched khams rnams mang po kun// byang chub sems dpa'i dkyil 'khor nyid// sa chu spyan
5b2(zha): dang mA ma ki/ me rlung gos dkar sgrol ma ste// nam mkha' dbyings kyi dbang phyug ma// srid gsum ye nas sangs rgyas zhing // thams cad ma lus chos su cog/ sangs
5b3(zha): rgyas nyid la gzhan ma yin// sangs rgyas nyid las gzhan pa'i chos// sangs rgyas nyid kyis mi brnyes so// zhes brjod pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes
5b4(zha): par gyur to// de nas btsun mo bya ba mo chos kun tu bzang mos/ bcom ldan 'das yid kun tu bzang po dang gnyis su med par gyur nas/ ched du brjod
5b5(zha): pa'i de brjod do// kye ma'o// phyogs bcu stong khams ye nas dben// srid pa gsum ni dag pa'i zhing // snyigs ma lnga ni bde ldan gnas// phung po lnga ni mngon
5b6(zha): sangs rgyas// thams cad mchog gi snying po bas// gzhan du rgyal ba'i chos mi btsal// nyid las gzhan zhes bya ba'i chos// rgyal bas btsal yang mi rnyed do// zhes
5b7(zha): brjod pas/ thams cad ye nas sangs rgyas par de bzhin gshegs pa nyid kyis mkhyen to// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ gleng bslang ba'i le'u ste gnyis
6a1(zha): pa'o// // de nas gnyis su med pa'i bdag nyid chen pos/ ye nas sangs rgyas pa'i sems ye shes su bskyed pa'i thabs
6a2(zha): 'di gsungs so// e ma'o ngo mtshar rmad kyi chos// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang // skye ba med las thams cad skyes// skyes pa nyid na skye bo med// e
6a3(zha): ma'o ngo mtshar rmad kyi chos// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kun gyi gas nga // 'gag pa med las thams cad 'gag/ zhagag pa nyid na 'gag pa med// e ma'o ngo mtshan rmad kyi
6a4(zha): chos// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang // gnas pa med las thams cad gnas// gnas pa nyid na gnas pa med// e ma'o ngo mtshar rmad kyi chos// rdzogs
6a5(zha): ba'i sangs rgyas kun gyi gsung // dmigs pa med las thams cad dmigs// dmigs pa nyid na dmigs pa med// e ma'o ngo mtshar rmad kyi chos// rdzogs pa'i sangs
6a6(zha): rgyas kun gyi gsapa// 'gro 'ong med las 'gro dang 'od// 'gro bang nyid na 'gro 'ong med// ces brjod pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / btsun mo'i tshogs thams
6a7(zha): cad mnyes pas khyab par gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / btsun mo'i tshogs dang bcas pas ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// e ma'i ye nas gsang ba'i

6b2(zha): thams cad ye nas sangs rgyas pa'i ngo bo nyid du gcig pa'i mtshan nyid yin pas dbyer med na/ thugs rje skyes nas byang chub tu 'gro ba'i rnam par rtog pa ma rig pa las/ 'gro ba lnga'i ris
6b3(zha): bsam gyis mi khyab par smin pa la/ thugs rje chen po'i sangs rgyas kyi ye shes chen po skyes nas/ ched du brjod pa'i nga brjod do// e ma'o bder gshegs snying po las//

6b5(zha): bcings med de// bcing bar bya ba'ang yod ma yin// rnam rtog po dag tu 'dzin pa yis/ nan gyis mkha' la mdud pa 'dor// bcings med rnam par grol med pa'i// ye nas
6b6(zha): lhun rdzogs sangs rgyas chos// bstan phyir spro ba sna tshogs mdzad// ces de bzhin gshegs pa nyid de bzhin gshegs pa nyid la ched du gleng ngo // gsang ba'i snying po de kho na
6b7(zha): nyid nges pa las/ don dam pa dang kun rdzob kyi byang chub kyi sems ye shes su bskyed pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams ca

7a3(zha): ba chen po bcom ldan 'das re res 'dus ba rnam pa bzhis 'gro ba lnga'i don mdzad de// bltam pa dang / rab tu byung ba dang / dka' thub mdzad pa dang / sangs rgyas pa
7a4(zha): dang / bdud btul ba dang / sa kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / tshe 'phrul chen po bsnun pa dang / mya ngan las 'angs pa la sogs pa rtson 'grub pa drug rnam pazhesam

10a6(zha): rgyud kyi rgyal po sgyu 'phrul dra ba las/ chos thams cad la chos nyid kyi rgyu yod pa dang / rigs brgyud chad pa dang / rigs brgyad so sor dbye ba'i mdo bshad pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// /
10a7(zha): / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dgongs pa gcig tu gyur nas/ mnyam pa chen po'i tshul rdo rje dbyings su chos thams cad ye nas sangs rgyas pa'i ting
10b1(zha): nge 'dzin las mi g.yo bar/ chos thams cad ming tsam du gnas pa'i yi ge 'phreng ba'i 'khor lo zhes bya ba 'di sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // a rab
10b2(zha): tu bstan 'gyur a dkar las// shin tu phra ba'i a rnams spro// phyogs kun khyab par gsal gyur nas// bsdus kyang 'phel 'grib med par bsten// de las ming tshogs
10b3(zha): gsal bar kun// spro zhing bsdu ba'ang de bzhin no// 'di ni dngos grub rdo rje yis// bstan 'byung ye shes rgyu yin no// a/ ka khag b+hung / tsa tsha dzadz+nyAnya/ Ta tha Da D+haH
10b4(zha): ta tha da d+ha na/ pa pha ba b+ham/ ya wa ral/ shawas ha/ k+Sha/ i I/ u U/ e ai/ o au/ 'di dag phyung bas 'jig rten drug gi phyogs bcu mtha' yas pa rnam pa drug
10b5(zha): tu g.yos/ rab tu g.yos/ kun tu g.yos nas/ chos thams cad ming gi mtshan nyid tsam du gnas par gyur to// hoH/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis ched du brjod pa
10b6(zha): 'di brjod do// a ni stong dang mi stong gis// dbu ma dbyings su yod ma yin// thams cad ming tsam sangs rgyas kun// yi ge 'phreng ba nyid la gnas// a nyid sna tshogs
10b7(zha): par snang ba'i// ka la sogs pa bzhi bcu gnyis// sgra yi ming gis thams cad 'dus// mngon rdzogs rgyal por bde ba'i gnas// e mngo mtshar ya mtshan gyis//
11a1(zha): 'phrul chen bzhi bcu rtsa lnga'i ming // tshig rnams ma lus 'joms pa'i gnas// sna tshogs rin chen rgyu bzhin ste// dngos med yi ge rang bzhin sems// /
11a2(zha): bdag med mtha' bral mi dmigs kyang // dbyibs dang kha dog ming tshogs kyis// rol pa cir yang sprul cing ston// phyogs bcu dus bzhir gshegs pa yi// ye shes sems
11a3(zha): dpa'i sku gsung thugs// dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu rtsa lnga nyid// yi ge mgo nas k+Sha la sogs// sems kyi rang bzhin yi ge ste// yi ge'i dngos po yod ma yin// dmigs med de/
11a4(zha): nyid sna tshogs pa'i// sku gsung thugs kyi dkyil 'khor che// sku gsung thugs kyi ngo mtshar gyis// ya mtshan 'khrul chen rab dgug pa'i// dbyings la dbyings kyis bris pa
11a5(zha): ste/ yi ge zhes ni de phyir brjod// mgon ma nor lam yin te// rting ni shes rab ming du smras// shad ni thams cad tshigs su gcod// a ni skye med de bzhin te// zan sgyu
11a6(zha): 'phrul rdo rje nyid// Ta ni snang ba'i sgyu 'phrul nyid// Ta ni sgyu 'phrul yid bzhin nyid// D+ha ni sgyu 'phrul rnam dag nyid// Na ni kun tu sgyu 'phrul nyid// tha ni dra bas mngon rdzogs nyid//
11a7(zha): ti ni dra bas bstan pa nyid// da ni dro bas lha ni nyid// d+hi ni dra bas 'khril ba nyid// nani dra bas kun tu 'gyur// ka ni spyan gyi thugs kyi mchog/ kha ni snyan gyi thugs kyi
11b1(zha): mchog/ ga ni shangs kyi thugs kyi mchog/ g+ha ni ljags kyi thugs kyi mchog/ nga ni thugs kyang 'jigs byed pa'o// tsa ni spyan gyi sku yi mchog/ tsha ni snyan gyi sku yi mchog/
11b2(zha): dza ni shangs kyi sku yi mchog/ dz+ha ni ljags kyi sku yi mchog/ nya ni sku yang 'jigs byed pa'o// pa ni spyan gyi gsung gi mchog/ pha ni snyan gyi gsung gi mchog/ ba ni shangs kyi
11b3(zha): gsung gi mchog/ b+ha ni ljags kyi gsung gi mchog/ ma ni gsung yang 'jigs byed pa'o// yini skye ba rnam par dag/ wa ni gnas pa dag pa yin// ra ni 'jigs pa dag pa ste//
11b4(zha): la ni stong bdag pa'o// sha ni rtag byed dag pa ste// ShA ni chad pa'ang yod pa yin// sa ni mtha' bral bdag med pa'o// ha ni mtshan ma med pa nyid// kla ni ye shes thugs kyi thugs//
11b5(zha): i ni rdul snyed lha rnams su// A ni rdul snyed lha ma yin// u ni rdul snyed mi rnams su// A ni rdul snyed byol song rnams// e ni rdul snyed yi dgas so// e ni rdul snyed
11b6(zha): dmyal ba rnams// oM ni thams cad 'jig par byed// oM ni thams cad zhig pa yin// yi go 'khor lo tshogs chen 'dis// sku gsung thugs kyi 'phreng bas bsdus// zhes
11b7(zha): brjod do// a ho/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa btsun mo'i tshogs dang gnyis su med pa'i dkyil 'khor de dag nyid kyis gsang ba 'di nyid// sku gsung thugs dang yon tan 'phrin la/
12a1(zha): rdo rje las phyung ngo // a ho/ thabs dang shes rab dgyes sprin byang chub sems tshogs rgyu 'khor lo// 'bras bu rgyal bzhin drug ngo mtshar ming tshogs bzhi bcu
12a2(zha): gnyis// 'dus ma byas nyid du dus byas rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor ba byin pa'i dam// 'da' bar mi mdzad dbang med rgyu rkyen tshogs pa'i mthu chen yin// a ho/ zhes rdo rje gsang
12a3(zha): ba'i tshig tu'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yi ge 'khor lor gyur to// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las// yi ge 'khor lo'i 'phreng ba bkod pa'i le'u ste drug
12a4(zha): pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rgyud kyi rgyal po sgyu 'phrul dra ba las shin tu gsang ba'i phyir/ gras sngags kyi rgyud phyi ma dang / nang pa thabs kyi rgyud
12a5(zha): gzhan las khams bco brgyad du bstan la/ gtsug lag thams cad lus kyang bco brgyad du brtan pa yin/ lung gi spyi 'di ni shin tu zab pa'i phyir/ khams nyi shu rtsa gcig tu
12a6(zha): bstan te/ lung gi spyi yang rgyud dang gsung rab thams cad 'byung ba'i rgyu yin/ gsang ba'i dbang po dang / gsang ba'i yul gnyis ka yang skye mched dang khams thams cad 'byung
12a7(zha): ba'i gzhi yin pa'i phyir/ shin tu gsang bar gsungs so// dkyil 'khor de dag shin tu gsal bar bstan pa'i phyir// nyid la nyid ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// skye
12b1(zha): ma ngo mtshar gsang ba'i chos// thams cad kun la rang bzhin gnas// ye nas dag mnyam ma rtogs pas// kun la yod cing rang bzhin gsang // gzhan du min la shin/
12b2(zha): tu gsang // don nyid kyi sa gsang ba'i rgyu// mnyam pa'i rdo rje can gyis gsungs// 'dri ni byang chub snying po mchog/ a ho gsang ba'i tshig tu'o// dbang po yul dus
12b3(zha): snang ba rnams// byang chub sems kyi dkyil 'khor nyid// phung po lnga dang 'byung ba lnga// rigs lnga yab yum bcu ru 'byor// skye mched khams rnams bcu drug po// byang
12b4(zha): chub sems dpa' sems ma yi// dkyil 'khor nyid kyi dbyings yin te// sems dpa' rdo rje gsang ba'i dbang // rdo rje gsang ba'i dbang po thabs// dbang po yul ni shes rab
12b5(zha): dbyings// dbang po'i thugs ni rdo rje'i sems// thams cad byang chub sems ma yi// rdo rje gsang ba'i dbang por 'dus// thams cad 'byung ba'i gtar nyid dang //
12b6(zha): thams cad 'gro ba'i gnas nyid de// de yis ma skyes gang yang myed// 'das dang ma 'das kun gyi rgyu// de las thams cad skye zhing 'byung // kun gyi phyag rgya rgyu yin te//
12b7(zha): bde ba'i byang chub grub pa'i rdzas// de las bskyed cing de las spro// dngos grub thams cad sgrub pa'i gnas// dbang po rdo rje pad+mar ldan// gnyis med byang chub sems
13a1(zha): 'phro na/ mi dmigs bde dang longs spyod 'phro// sku gsung thugs dang ye shes lnga// gsang ba'i lha mo bzhi rnams dang // mchod pa'i lha mo rdzogs
13a2(zha): ldan pa na// 'jug dang ldan dang gnas pa dang // smon pa'i byang chub sems yin no// g.yo dang bskyod dung ldan dang gnas// 'gug dang 'dzin dang de bzhin te// bsdus
13a3(zha): dang 'khril pa'i don bsgrub phyir// bsdum dang mi gtong dbang sgyur te// bde ba'i dgra snyan phyogs bcur sgrog/ shin tu sgeg pa'i gzi brjid 'bar// yid bzhin rin chen
13a4(zha): 'phreng ba 'bar// dbyangs snyan yid 'i phrog gzi ldan 'bar// gzugs mdzes bskyod pas phyogs bcur g.yo// kun tu tshim byed brog sung thim// lha mdzes rin
13a5(zha): chen phung po 'phro// 'od gsal 'phro bas kun tu'i bar// bdud rtsi bsil rdo 'jam pa'i dbyings// a la la ho/ gsang dbang pad+mar ldan gyur nas// chags
13a6(zha): ba med pa'i tshul gyis su// pha rol phyin bcu rgyu'abras rdzogs// sa bcu rim gyis bgrod med rdzogs// kun tu 'od gsal pad+ma'i spyan yang rdzogs// yi ge 'phreng
13a7(zha): ba 'khor lo bsam mi khyab// thabs dang shes rab sa yang rdzogs// yang dag rdzogs chen thabs dang ldan// shes rab bla med yang dag rdzogs// bsod nams
13b1(zha): ye shes tshogs chen rdzogs par rol// a la la ho/ de bzhin nyid kyi gsang mchog las// khams ni nyi shu rtsa gcig ste// bco brgyad po ni rgyud gzhan bzhin//
13b2(zha): gsum ni de bzhin kun gyi bdag/ bco brgyad 'byung ba'i gnas yin te// byang chub bsgrub pa'i gzhi yang yin// bde ba'i byin pa'i rgyu yin te// gsang ba'i mtshan nyid
13b3(zha): rjod pa ni// dbang po rdo rje gsang ba'i rgyal// yul ni pad+ma'i bde mchog dbyings// sems ni byang chub 'byung ba'i gter// dbang po yul sems ldan gyur na//
13b4(zha): gsang ba mchog gi 'phrul chen spro// dkyil 'khor rdul snyed grangs med dang // phun sum tshogs pa'i lhun grub rnams// gsang ba dbang mchog 'byin par byed//
13b5(zha): 'di ni rtswa gcig yin par gsungs// gsang ba'i don mchog 'di dgra ni// lta ba dman la bshad byas na// dus min par ni srog zad nas// mgo 'gas snying
13b6(zha): yang 'tshig par 'gyur// kha ba len gyis ni lcags sdud ltar// mi 'dod bzhin du dbang med par// ngan song skal bar ltung bar 'gyur// de bas 'di ni shin tu gsang //
13b7(zha): shes rab rgya chen blo za ba yangs pa yi// blo bstan snying rje dang ldan dang // rang bzhin ngang tshul bzang la bstan// gzhan du sbyin par bya ba min// zhes nyid la yang nyid rjod
14a1(zha): de/ shin tu zab pa'i phyir bsgyur te/ gzhan du ma bshad do// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor khams nyi
14a2(zha): shu rtsa gcig tu bsdus nas/ thams cad ma lus pa r-i dri byings su bsdus pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// // / de nas yi ge 'khor lo sprin bkod pa las/ sgyu
14a3(zha): 'phrul rnam par spros pa 'di brjod do// rtsa ba med pa'i sems nyid ni// chos rnams kun gyi rtsa ba yin// sems nyid yi ge'i rang bzhin te// yi ge yid bzhin rin chen
14a4(zha): yin// sgyu 'phrul dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu gnyis// dra ba'i dkyil 'khor mngon rdzogs pas// phyogs bcu dus bzhi mngon rdzogs pa'i// dkyil 'khor thams cad grub
14a5(zha): par 'gyur// bdud rtsir 'gyur zhing 'byung ba dang // bzhi brgya rtsa bzhind sel zhing // longs spyod 'byung zhing ngan song sbyong // spyir yang gzhan du 'gyur bar bsgrub// nam
14a6(zha): mkha' rdo rje sra 'byung zhing // 'bar nis me lhung 'tshig pa dang // chur 'gyur 'bab pa'ang de bzhin to// 'jig rten khams ni gtor ba dang // thams cad ltung zhing
14a7(zha): stongs par 'gyur// 'gug dang gtang dang bcing dang dgrol// gso dang bsad dang pha ma dang rgyal// ting 'dzin 'di yis byed par 'gyur// de nyid ye shes rang snang ba//
14b1(zha): ming tshig gzugs mchog yid bzhin gyis// mun pa snang byung ji bzhin du// 'gyur bas gser 'gyur sman gyi tshul// ston pa mchog brtson rtog pa gsal//
14b2(zha): dam tshig sngags dang phyag rgya rnams// mnyams shes shing yo byad ldan// 'grub 'gyur mi ldan don med blag/ dus gsum rgyal bas thugs chud pa'i// dngos grub
14b3(zha): mchog gi snying po ni// zad pa'i dus med yid bzhin mdzod// 'phel 'grib med par 'byung ba ste// dngos po med las dngos po'i sprin// sna tshogs rnam par 'byung/
14b4(zha): zhing 'gyur// dngos rnams nyid na dngos med pa// rtog pa'i dbang sgyur ting 'dzin yin// grang gis dmigs med mi shes pa// de yis chos kyi dbyings mi shes// /
14b5(zha): de phyir dngos dang dngos med pa// 'jigs pas dmigs med shes par gyis// gzhi rtsa med pa'i sems nyid ni// pho mo ma yin ma ning min// mtshan med ma yin rigs/
14b6(zha): rgyud min// kha dog ma yin dbyibs ma yin// gnas su ma yin gang yang med// de bzhin nyid dbyings ye shes te// thabs kyi phyag rgya kun gyi rgyu// thabs las
14b7(zha): thabs byung thabs bsam yas// tha dad min la tha dad pa'i// nang dang nang gi phyi rol gyi// dkyil 'khor bsam yas ye shes rol// 'jigs med kun bzang phyag rgya'i
15a1(zha): mchog/ gang gis glang chen spros 'dra'i sems// mnyam par gzhag pas btul nas su// sngags dang phyag rgya rab bstan na// dngos grub ya
15a2(zha): mtshan chen por 'gyur// zhes brjod pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa nyid gzigs mos mnyes par gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dang / gsung dang / thugs
15a3(zha): rdo rje las rtog pa'i tshig 'di phyung ngo // e ma'o snying po la ma bcas pas// 'jigs med dbyings nyid kun bzang phyag rgya'i mchog/ rang bzhin sku gsung thugs chen
15a4(zha): papo/ byang chub lhun grub bdal bu'i dang // snying po nyid ni snying por kun bcas kun tu gnas// de nyid rdzogs pa'i ngad las dngos grub kun shar kun tu gnas//
15a5(zha): ho/ rdo rje ga sang ba'i tshig tu'o// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ sgyu 'phrul ba sgrub pa'i ting 'dzin gyi le'u ste brgyad pa'o// /
15a6(zha): de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rgyud kyi rgyal po sgyu 'phrul dra ba rung bzhin gyi dkyil 'khor las/ lhag pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi dkyil 'khor gyis sngags 'chang rnams lhar ba sgrub pa'i
15a7(zha): dkyil 'khor 'di don yod par bya ba'i phyir/ ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// e ma'o ye nas rnam dag pa'i// thabs dang shes rab ldan par gnas// byang chub mchog
15b1(zha): tu nyi zla 'char// de nyid bzhugs gnas yin par gsungs// chos rnams thams cad gnyis med pa'i// dbyings su thim pa'i 'od zer gsal// gcig dang
15b2(zha): spros pa thams cad med// gcig dang du mar bral ba'i phyir// dkyil 'khor spros med zlum po'i tshul// ye na sa mya ngan 'das pa'i tshogs// ye shes rgyu dang 'a bras
15b3(zha): bur ldan// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes sku// chos kyi 'khor lo yongs kyis bskor// thugs rjes byin rlabs spros pa yis// ye shes bzhi yi dkyil 'khor
15b4(zha): zlo/ ye shes lnga dang sku gsung thugs// byin rlabs ya mtshan bsam mi khyab// rang snang ba yi thabs las byung // bsod namras ye shes tshogs rdzogs pa'i//
15b5(zha): thugs rjes rgyas pa'i gzhal yas khang // mtha' dbus med par rgyas par gnas// stong smon mtshan med 'od gsol 'jug/ de phyir ye shes sgo bzhir shar// der
15b6(zha): 'gro la ma stegs brgyad dang ldan// rang bzhin ye nas 'od gsal phyir// nyi zla brtsegs pa'i gdan khri 'bar// yen sa rnam par dag pa'i phyir// ma chags pad+ma 'bar
15b7(zha): ba'i gdan// zad med ye shes stor gyur pas// yid bzhin rin chen 'bar ba'i gdan// ye nas mnyam nyid mi bda'i phyir// ta la'i ljon shing rang bzhin gnas//
16a1(zha): rab yid bzhin bskod pa'i phyir// dpag bsam shing gis rin chen 'bar// yid bzhin rin chen rgyan gyis bskor// thams cad la ni dbang /
16a2(zha): sgyur phyir// 'jig rten lha chen rnams kyis bskor// gsung ba de nyid nges pa las// sgyu 'phrul bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis kyis// thams cad lha nyid rtag tu sbyor/
16a3(zha): thams cad ma lus dkyil 'khor mchog/ 'dis ni rang bzhin dkyil 'khor dang // gzugs brnyan lhag pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum// ting 'dzin lhag pa'i
16a4(zha): dkyil 'khor dag/ byang chub sems dang tshogs mchog rten// zhes nyid la nyid bshad do// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ shin tu gsang ba'i
16a5(zha): dkyil 'khor bsdus nas// lha'i gzugs brnyan bstan pa'i le'u ste dgu pa'o// / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rang bzhin gci
16a6(zha): dang du ma med pa'i bdag nyid thams cad kyis/ 'jig rten drug gi phyogs bcu thams cad la nyid kyis mtshan che ba'i dkyil 'khor dbyung bar bzhed nas/ ched du brjod pa
16a7(zha): 'di brjod do// ye shes phyogs bzhi dbus rtag ste// dkyil 'khor bsam las lhun grub ni// rdzogs chen rtogs pa'i rnal 'byor pas// kun 'byung dkyil
16b1(zha): 'khor chen por spyod// 'khor lo rtsubs bzhi mu khyud bcas// gru chad bzhis brgyan par khyams dang // kun tu gru bzhi sgo khyud ldan// rol mo sna tshogs
16b2(zha): sprin phung bzhin// dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu gnyis kyis brgyun// seng ge glang chen rta dang khyud// nam mkha' lding gi khri chen la// nyi zla pad+ma rin po che// gdan
16b3(zha): la rdzogs dang sems dpa'i tshul// 'khor lo rgyal po rgyal mo dang // g.yas nas mthong thos snom pa dang // myong dang btsun mo'i tshogs su bcas// gru char la ni
16b4(zha): mthong byed dang // thos byed snom byed myong byed rnams// btsun mo'i tshogs dang ldan par gnas// bar khyams la ni thub drug dang // mdun dang rgyab tu byed pa dang // bya ba
16b5(zha): ngag ni gnas par bstan// sgo khyud bzhi la 'joms pa ni// btsun mo'i tshogs dang ldan par gnas// rdo rje 'khor lo rin po che// pad+ma ral gri dril bu'abar//
16b6(zha): ud pa la klu shing la sogs mtshon// mdzes tshul mnyes pa'i yo byad 'dzin// mthing kha dkar po ser le brgan// ljang khu la sogs sna tshogs pa'i//
16b7(zha): mnyan lcug 'khril ldem gzhon tshul can// gsal mcher lhun stug gzi byin ldan// 'od zer 'phro ba'i tshogs chen po// 'bar ba'i 'phreng bas 'khrigs pa
17a1(zha): ste/ mtha' dbus med par khyab pa yi// dkyil 'khor bsam yas lhun gyis grub// sku yi phyag rgya che mchog ni// de bzhin dbyings
17a2(zha): la sam g.yos kyang // yang dag thar pa'i gzugs sku dang // 'gro ba ma lus gdul ba'i phyir// mthun byas sku ni sna tshogs ston// ston nyid sgyu ma migayor tshul//
17a3(zha): tshul nyid dbyings las g.yos pa med// ma g.yos bzhin du sna tshogs pa'i// de'i tshe mi mthun sna tshogs la// so sor 'dra bar snang ba ni// de bzhin nyid kyis ma
17a4(zha): bcos kyang // las 'phro bang gi so sor snang // dper na me ling chu zla bzhin// de'i tshe 'gre drug thams cad la// sdig spong gzugs su snang b.ru bstan// dge tshul
17a5(zha): rnams la dgra bcom gzugs// rang rgyal rnams la bse ru'i tshul// gzhan yang theg mchog rim pa bzhin// 'og min bla med gnas mchog tu// sku ni rnam
17a6(zha): snang mdzad chul// byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor rnams la// de bzhin gsung mchog mi smra ste// sku yi chos rnams 'jal bar ston// me long bstan pa'i tshul bzhin
17a7(zha): du// dngos kyis mdog ngan thams cad sel// 'khor gyis de bzhin sku bltas na// byang chub sgrib pa gting dpag med// le long bzhin du skul snang // de nas sa
17b1(zha): bcu rims kyis 'byung // bla med byang chub yang dag 'thob// chos sku dpag med brjod du med// longs spyod zad med rin chen gter// sprul pa bye ba bsam mi khyab//
17b2(zha): mtshan dang dpe byad thams cad rdzogs// spyod yul kun tu ma 'das pa// tshogs chen gnyis kyang rdzogs par ro lo// thabs dang shes rab sa yi mchog/ de la sogs
17b3(zha): te bas ma yas mchog/ skye 'chi med pa'i g.yung drung sku// nyon mongs kun gyi zhing du gnas// zad med shes kyi gter du gyur// rdo rje rig pa 'dzin pa'i sku// thams
17b4(zha): cad dbyer med mnyam pa'i sku// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes sku// de'i tshe sku lnga kun kyang rdzogs// zhes brjod pas/ 'jig rten drug gi phyogs bcu mtha' yas
17b5(zha): mu med pa thams cad du/ dkyil 'khor brjod kyis mi lang bzhing gi rdul snyed cig gsal bar gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa btsun mo'i tshogs dang gnyis su med pa'i
17b6(zha): yon tan chen po'i dkyil 'khor de dag nyid kyis gsang ba 'di nyid// sku gsung thugs dang yon tan 'phrin las rdo rje las phyung ngo // a ho/ dmigs bya dmigs med mi dmigs dpag
17b7(zha): med bsam mi khyab// ye shes rang rig dkyil 'khor sna tshogs brjod mi leng // mnyam dang mi mnyam kun khyab khyab med khyab pa'i dbyings// ye nas kun gsal dkyil
18a1(zha): 'khor rnams 'phro spros pa med// ye nas kun khyab dkyil 'khongs ma yas zhing gi rdul snyed du// ye nas rnam spros snying po kun gnas gnas pa med//
18a2(zha): a ho/ zhes rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig tu'o// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ dkyil 'khor spros pa'i le'u ste bcu pa'o// // de nas de
18a3(zha): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyam pa nyid la bzhugs nas/ 'khor bsam gyis mi khyab pa thams cad kyang / nyid la nyid mnyes par mchod par mchod cing // kun tu
18a4(zha): bzang po dgyes te/ phyogs bcu rus bzhi ma lus pa thams cad kyi bzhugs gnas gzhal yas khang / rin po che sna tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ tshad dpag tu med pa
18a5(zha): rgyas pa mtha' dbus med par khyab cing / 'od zer sgrib pa med par rang byung ba la bzhugs nas/ ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// nyid kyi dbyings nyid 'phro ba tshad dpag
18a6(zha): med/ kun nas dkyil 'khor yongs su ma chad pa'i// srid gsum yang dag mnyam sbyor spyod yul te// mtshan 'dzin 'das pa mchog gi rgyu la byung // dbang sgyur shin
18a7(zha): tu rnam par dag pa yi// de bzhin gshegs pa 'og min gnas bzhugs nas// gzung 'dzin bral ba'i bla med rjes 'dod dang // 'jig rten 'khor gyis bcos kun
18b1(zha): dbang phyug dang // gzhan yang 'jig rten phyogs bcu khams gnas pa// bdud rtsi ro yi dga' ba bde chen thob// dug gsum dri bral bdud sde tshar bcad pa'i// 'das
18b2(zha): dang ma 'das de bzhin nyid du sbyor// shes rab thabs ldan nges pa'i don 'byung ba// rig pa'i thabs chen dbang phyug nyid du bsgom// stong smon mtshan med rang bzhin 'od
18b3(zha): gsal ba'i// zad med bsod nams tshogs kyis brgyan par 'gyur// b+h+rUM rang byung nyin pad+ma rin chen rgyas la bzhugs// rdo rje mnyam nyid thugs su chud pa yi// mnyam
18b4(zha): rdzogs chen po'i lhun la rol pa mdzad// bde gshegs nyid dbyings de bzhin nyid gnas pa// dus bzhi rgyal ba kun dang mnyam par 'u ba// thams cad 'od gsal dkyil 'khor
18b5(zha): thugs chud pa'i// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje 'chang las byung // spyod yul 'phro med brjod kyis mi lang ba'i// dus bzhi mnyam nyid nges pa'i don nyid nyon// thugs rje'i
18b6(zha): dbang gis 'gro drug dus gnas bzhugs// nga dang bdag med mnyam pa'i dbyings mkhyen pa// mnyam pa'i don grub rdo rje can gyis bya// rnam par rtog med byang chub rdo rje'i
18b7(zha): / shes rab mchog gi sa ma lus yongs sdud pa// bder gshegs mi gnas mnyam nyid ngang du byon// thabs chen ma 'dres rnam par thar pa yi// dmigs med
19a1(zha): bder gshegs nyid dbyings thugs chud pa// thabs dang shes rab dbyings nyid dam pa'i mchog/ phyogs bcu dus bzhi dbyings nas mthar gtugs pa//
19a2(zha): rang rig rgyal po che yis rtog par 'gyur// shes rab mchog ldan gsal ba'i ngang 'chang ba// thugs rje'i byin rlabs sna tshogs gsang 'phro ba'i// bde gshegs ma lus
19a3(zha): thams cad 'byung ba'i gnas// yid bzhin rin chen mi zad par ldan 'phro// gzhal yas khang de ltar yang dbu bas so// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/
19a4(zha): gzhal yas khang dbub pa'i thabs 'dra ba'i le'u ste bcu gcig pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa btsun mo'i tshogs dang bcas pa thams cad kyis
19a5(zha): sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje la sa'i'ad dag phyung ngo // bruM bi shwa bi shud+d+he/ hUM badz+ra d+h+r-i ka/ swa rat+na d+h+r-i ka/ aM a ro l-i ka/ ha pradz+nyA d+hI ka/ muM d+he shwa ra d+he/ lam
19a6(zha): te shwa ra ti/ mAM mo ha ra ti/ byaM ra ga ra ti/ haM ba ti/ k+ShI rang ya/ traM a ra ra yaM/ hi pad+ma d+haM ma/ dzi ku ra pi na ha/ hUM la s+ye sa ma ya s+t+waM/ tr-i mA le sa ma ya ho/ hri gI tI ra
19a7(zha): ho haM/ a ni ra tir ho ya mau/ me dar ni swA hA/ b+h+yAM ni sa raM ba swA hA/ hUM sAM rats+tsha ya sa hA/ muM shri aM ra g+ha sA hA/ dza d+hA pa pra be sha/ hUM puSh+pa A be sha/ bi dI pa su ki ni/
19b1(zha): / ho ga na d+he tsid tra/ hUM la mAn+ta k+Shid phaT/ hU big+h+nAn ta kra ta phaT/ pad+man+ta k+Shita phaT/ hUM/ pradz+nyAn+ta krita phaT/ oM ma hA badz+ra d+hA ra ma ha kro d+hi shwa rI dz+wa la ni phaT/ oM ma hA rat+na d+ha ra
19b2(zha): / ma hA kro d+hi shwa ri dz+wa la ni phaT/ oM ma hA pad+ma d+ha rA ma hA kro d+hi shwa ri dz+wa la ni phaT/ oM ma hA karma d+ha ra ma ha kro d+hi shwa rI dz+wa la ni phaT/ hUM hUM hUM/ badz+ra tsit+ta hUM/ a a a/ badz+ra pa
19b3(zha): tras man ta oM/ oM mu ne kring swA hA/ oM mu ne truM swA hA/ oM mu ne sru ma swA hA/ oM mu ne b+h+raM swA hA/ oM mu ne k+ShaM swA hA/ oM mu na ye swA hA/ oM e h+ye hi b+ha ga ba na/ mA hA ka/
19b4(zha): rU Ni ka dr-i sh+yats+tsha/ sa ma ya s+t+wa~M/ dzaHhUM bi ho/ oM AHhUM swA hA/ babab ba ba/ dzA dzA dzAdzA/ sa sa sa s+yAs/ ma ma ma ma ma/ ya ya ya ya ya/ oM
19b5(zha): hUM swA hA/ oM badz+ra sa ma ya oM/ badz+ra sa ma ya AM/ badz+ra sa ma ya hUM/ badz+ra sa ma ya traM/ badz+ra s+yA ma ya haM/ oM/ ye shes rgyal po sku gsung thugs// yon tan
19b6(zha): 'phrin las rmad po che// de nyid du ni mnyam sbyor ba'i// phyag rgya chen por ba dag sbyor cig/ oM badz+ra sa ma ya hUM// oM badz+ra sa ma ya s+t+waM/ oM badz+ra sa ma ya ho/
19b7(zha): hUM baM ho/ zhes brjod pas/ gsung gi dkyil 'khor 'di dag gis/ 'jig rten drug gi phyogs bcu thams cad khyab par grags so// rab tu grags so// kun tu
20a1(zha): grags so// gsang ba'i snying po de khon nyid nges pa las/ gsang sngags kyi le'u ste bcu gnyis pa'o// // de nas bcom
20a2(zha): ldan 'das byed pa po rdo rje dang / bya ba mo rdo rje gnyis su med pa'i dkyil 'khor la thim par mdzad do// de nas phyogs bcu dus gsum gyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i bdag nyid chen
20a3(zha): pos/ bdag nyid chen po'i ye shes dang byin rlabs bsdu ba zhes bya ba 'di/ sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje sgyu 'phrul dra ba las phyung ngo // oM ma hA shu n+ya ta dz+nyA na badz+ra swa b+hA
20a4(zha): babA Ad ma ko&haM/ oM ma hA a d+ha ri sha dz+nyA na badz+ra swa b+hA ba a dA ma kota haM/ oM ma hA pra be sha dz+nyA na badz+ra swa b+ha ba Ad ma kota haM/ oM ma hA sa man ta dz+nyA na badz+ra swa b+ha ba A da ma kod+hats+tsha
20a5(zha): / oM ma hA kri ta a nut+ta ra dz+nyA na badz+ra swa b+hA ba Ad ma ko&haM/ oM sarba ta thA ga ta ma hA kA ya badz+ra swa b+hA ba Ad ma ko&haM/ oM sarba ta thA ga ta ma hA bAk+ka badz+ra swa b+ha ba A da ma kota ha/ oM sarba
20a6(zha): ta thA gA ta ma hA tsit+ta badz+ra swa b+hA ba Ad ma ko \u0f85ha/ oM sarba ta thA gA ta ma hA ra ga na badz+ra swa b+hA ba A da ma kot+ka haM/ oM sarba ta thA ga ta ma hA pu tsa badz+ra swa b+ha baM A da ma ko&haM/ zhes brjod
20a7(zha): pas thim par 'gyur/ gsal bar gyur/ 'bar 'gyur to// e ma 'ongo mtshar rmad kyi chos// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kun gyis gsung // sgra dang ming tshig kun
20b1(zha): las 'das// sna tshogs rnams gsas par 'byung // kasra gcig dkyil 'khor lan lagan// bsam gyis mi byu kun tu byug// sgra dang med tshig so sor gas/
20b2(zha): thams cad gsung gi phyag rgya'i mchog/ rgyud mchog sgyu 'phrul dra ba las// bde ldan gsung gi don byung ba// thams cad pad+ma'i ngang gyur na// grol thar lam dang 'khor ba'i
20b3(zha): sgra// ji skad brjod kyang gsung mchog skye// theg pa mtho dman thams cad dang // log 'gro ma lus thams cad skad// byang chub rdo rje'i gsung du bsdus// bsdus nyid

20b5(zha): dper na de bzhin sbrid bsangs bzhin// gsung gcig sgra yis thams cad go/ 'di ni gsung mchog rgyal po yin// theg pa mtho dman bsam lus kyang // de bzhin nyid
20b6(zha): las ma gsungs te// gdul bya'i thabs su so sor go/ de ltar gsung rab kun brjod kyang // de bzhin nyid kyis gsungs pa med// yi ge med dang rig pa'i gsung // /
20b7(zha): ljags kyi rtse mor ma phyung yang // thugs rjes gsung gi byin brlabs kyis// 'gro don sna tshogs so sor gsal// gsal nyid gsung rdo rje mchog/ de bzhin gsung
21a1(zha): gi 'gro don rnams// de bzhin dang las ma g.yos kyang // dper na brag cha'i sgra bzhin no// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ dkyil
21a2(zha): 'khor byin pa sdu ba'i/ gsang sngags kyi le'u ste bcu gsum pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pas/ nyid kyi phyag rgya ston
21a3(zha): pa'i snying po zhes bya ba 'di/ ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// oM hUM badz+ra sa ta hU/ badz+ra pra ma na hUM/ muM badz+ra ga na d+ha huM/ oM tsakra ma N+Da la o/ la badz+ra gan d+ha ba sha lalaM/
21a4(zha): s+yAM ra da na pra ba ni sa~M/ oM badz+ra ga na d+ha pa sha o/ oM pad+ma pra b+ha na a/ phyi badz+ra gan d+ha pra b+hanA bya/ ha khA da ga tik+Sh+Na pra b+hA haM/ taM badz+ra g+han d+hu ba sha pra b+han tAM/ k+ShI ra dan pra b+han
21a5(zha): k+ShI/ hUM badz+ra g+han d+ha pra b+hAn pA sha hUM/ tra kha dag pra b+ha na tra/ tra badz+ra g+han d+hU pa sha pra b+han tra/ nr-i preng+ga pra b+hA na dzi/ hriM badz+ra gan d+ha ba sha ha pu na hr-i/ ha badz+ra pra b+han ha/ a badz+ra gan d+ha
21a6(zha): pr-i b+ha sha pra b+ha na a/ me ka la pra b+ha na ha me/ hUM badz+ra ga na d+ha pre ba na ba sha hUM/ b+h+r-i pra ba na ma la b+d+hi/ swaM badz+ra gan d+ha ba sha ha pu ba kha na sa/ hu rad na swa sa ti sa tra pu ba na sAM/ hri
21a7(zha): badz+ra gan d+ha ba sha pra b+ha na hri/ muM ud pa la ni pra b+ha na mu/ a badz+ra gan d+ha ba sha pra b+hi na a/ phaT badz+ra ya ma mud ga ra pra b+ha na phaT phaT/ oM badz+ra gan d+ha ba sha pra b+hi na o au/ phaT
21b1(zha): ma ha badz+ra pra b+ha na phaT phaT/ hUM ma hA ra da na badz+ra gan d+ha pa sha pra b+ha na hUM hUM/ phaT hri pad+ma mud ga ra pra b+ha na hI hri/ aM ma hA badz+ra pad+ma badz+ra ga na d+ha ba sha pra b+ha na hI hri/ a ka ra ma mu dag
21b2(zha): ra badz+ra pra b+ha na phaT phaT/ a ka ra ma badz+ra ga na d+ha ba sha pra ba na hU/ a a a/ zhes brjod pas/ phyag rgya gsung gi dkyil 'khor kun tu gsal bar gyur to// 'bar
21b3(zha): bar gyur to// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ don dam pa dang kun rdzob kyi byang chub kyi sems las phyag rgya gsung gi dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa'i le'u ste bcu bzhi
21b4(zha): pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rgyud kyi rgyal po sgyu 'phrul dra ba bstan pa las/ chos thams cad nam mkha' mkha' dang yum gyi mtshan nyid du
21b5(zha): 'dus par bstan nas/ ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// yang dag don gyi gsang mchog ni// bde ba thugs kyi dkyil 'khor la// nges pa'i don chen bzhi bcu gnyis//
21b6(zha): yid bzhin rin chen gsal 'bar thim// a thams cad ma lus thig le'i dbyings// sku lnga'i 'od zer mang po kun// thams cad yum gyur dbyings su thim// gsal
21b7(zha): 'bar sprin gyi bdag por 'gyur// byang chub sems kyi thig pa ni// kun la khyab cing mi gnas pa// kha dog gnas dang dbyibs ma yin// yon tan mchog gi snying po ni//
22a1(zha): rtog ge'i spyod yul yong ma yin// zab cing rgya cher rab sbyangs pa'i// gsal ldan brten pa'i spyod yul te// gzhan nas btsal zhing lhag tu med//
22a2(zha): thams cad nam mkha'i mtshan nyid de// sna tshogs 'jig rten khams g.yo dang // rgyal ba mngon byung thams cad kun// nam mkha'i dbyings su ma gyur pa// dus bzhi phyogs
22a3(zha): bcu yang med de// dus gsum bde gshegs nyid mi mnga'// sngon gyi bder gshegs thugs chud pa'i// nam mkha'i ngang du thams cad thim// thams cad shis
22a4(zha): rab dbyings nyid de// dbyings la dbyings ni rnam par sbyor// shes rab dbyings nyid sbyor ba yis// byang chub rdo rje thig le yin// dkyil 'khor bsam yas lhun grub
22a5(zha): dang / rgya dang bral ba'i gzhal yas kyis// kun la khyab cing mi gnas par// yon tan mchog gi gnas yan te// ma bcos rgyun gyi skad cig ma// de yi sa ma byas
22a6(zha): gang yang med// rang gi rnam rtog ma yin pa// yang dag gshegs dang log rtog dang // gzhan yang sprul pa mang po'i tshogs// phyogs bcu ma lus thams cad kyis//
22a7(zha): de la bsad cing gzung du med// kha dog dbyibs dang gnas ma yin// skyes bu dam pa mchog 'dod pas// de la rtag 'grus gsal bar gyis// de yi 'bras bu mtha
22b1(zha): phyin ni// rgyu 'bras med pa'i dus cig ste// thams cad ming tsam mtshan nyid du// yi ge 'bru gsum rdzogs par 'gyur// mi zad rgyan gyi 'khor lor gyur// tshogs
22b2(zha): tshon gnyis kyang rdzogs par rol// skye 'jig med pa'i dbyings la bzhugs// 'jig rten 'das dang 'jig rten pa'i// mtha' yas 'jig rten thams cad kun//
22b3(zha): rgyal ba yum gyi dbyings su thim// thams cad ma lus chos skur 'dus// ho gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ chos thams cad ming gi mtshan nyid de yum gyis

22b6(zha): nyid nges pa yi// snying po'i phyag rgya 'da' bar dka'// mi bskyod nyi ma'i dkyil yi ge/ rin chen zla ba'i dkyil yi ge/ lnga gnyis zung du spros pa las// sbyar
22b7(zha): ba phyag rgya 'byung ba'i rgyu// hUM dang mu gnyis rtse sbyar te// 'bru brgyad bsnol nas rtse sprad pas// rgyal ba kun dang mnyam sbyor ba'i// bde ba chen po sbyin pa'i rgya/
23a1(zha): 'bru bzhi sbas nas thugs ka ra ba kan// hUM bsgrengs rtse mor rdo rje 'bar// zla brtul 'bru sbas dril gsil zhing // 'khril ba'i tshul gyis chos

23a7(zha): bsgrengs rtse mor pad+mo 'bar// zla brtul 'bru sbas dril gsil zhing // 'khril ba'i tshul gyis chos la bsten// 'bru bzhi sbas nas thugs kar bkan// byaM bsgrengs rtse
23b1(zha): mor dril ga sil 'bar// nyi mA 'bru ldulas su 'khril// btud de 'dzum pa'i mdangs kyis lta// 'bru bzhi sbas nas thugs kar bkan// ha~M gi rtse mor ralA gr-i

23b4(zha): bo rdo rje 'bar// chos kyi 'khor lo rin chen ste// gzugs mdzes rin chen 'phreng ba dang // pi wa dgar mkhan mchog nyid de// me tog 'phreng dang spos mchod ma//

23b6(zha): dbyings kyi ngang du 'khril// sgo bzhi khro bo'i phyag rgya ni// nr-i mgo gdengs dang rdo rjes gnon/ thodra sbrul chen pos gnon pa dang // rdo rje rgya gram las kyis gnon//

24a1(zha): yin no// sreg par dang ni pi wang dang // go cha po ti rin chen sgrom// me dang chur ni rab tu bstan// yum ni dmigs med chos kyi dbyings//
24a2(zha): kun bzang mnyam gzhag ye shes 'phro// yum 'gyur mnyam rdzogs pad+ma'i dkyil// gzhan yang phyag rgya sna tshogs te// yang na de bzhin gshegs nyid do//
24a3(zha): yang na rdo rje thal mo nyid// mthe bong mdzub mo rdo rje 'dzin// myathe bong gung mo rgyal ba 'dzin// sprin lag mthe bong chags pa che// mthe'u chung mthe bong legs pa mchog
24a4(zha): dza hUM ba ho/ mdzub mo gnyis sbyar rin chen mchog/ gung mo gnyis sbyar gzi brjid don// srin lag gnyis sbyar rgyal ba'i tog/ bzhad pa'i dgra ni mthe'u chung sprad//
24a5(zha): tAM steng du ha/ mdzub mo steng 'og chos kyi mchog/ gud mo steng 'og 'jam dpal mchog/ srin lag steng 'og 'khor lo mchog/ mthe'u chung steng 'og sgra gsung yin//
24a6(zha): hU~Mb+ha tra~M haM/ mdzub mo rgyam ma lus kyi mchog/ gung mo rgyusam bsrung bar byos// srin lag tu glum gnod sbyin mchog/ mthe'u chung rgya gram gnas par bshad// hadz+ra a
24a7(zha): baM phyag rgya brda tshig chen po 'dis// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor mdzes par snang // rang bzhin dkyil 'khor phun sum tshogs// glu gnyis phyag rgya ldan pa yis// sa
24b1(zha): ler gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor 'bebs// phyag rgya spros pa chen pos ni// gzung dang 'dzin la rnam gnyis po// dag par gsal bas phyag rgya yin// yi ge so sor
24b2(zha): gsal ba yis// gar du bsgyur bas mya ngan 'das// dza dang ho la sogs pa yis// gar du bsgyur bas rdo rje 'chang // phyag rgya chen po che mchog ni// thabs dang
24b3(zha): shes rab rnal 'byor te// mi bskyod mau bskul thams cad kyang // phyag rgya chen po'i ngang du gnas// yan lag bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis ldan// de nyid yan lag spros
24b4(zha): bdag ste// bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis gsum 'phros 'gyur// de ltar ldan pa'i gtso mchog gis// rgyal ba rgyal mchog de bzhin du// dbu gnyis drug gis 'od 'phro bar//
24b5(zha): de la sogs te bsam mi khyab// phyogs bcu dus bzhi bas ma yas su// gdul ba'i don rnams so sor ston// theg pa mtho dman thams cad dang // phyen ci
24b6(zha): log rnams bsam yas dang // zhi khro'i tshogs chen thams cad la// so sor 'thun byas sna tshogs snang // dper na gar mkhan nyid 'dra ba// lus las mgos
24b7(zha): thams cad ston// mdor na phyag rgya thams cad ni// 'di zhes gcig ces brjod du med// gnyis dang gsum du rnam par 'phros// bskyod dang spro ba de bzhin nyid//
25a1(zha): mdor na bskul bskyod thams cad kun// phyag rgya chen po'i ngang du gnas// gnas nyid mi gnas gnas pa min// de skad dag mchog nyid kyis

27b1(zha): gsung thugs kyi ye shes ni// las kyi sems dpa' dpa' bo yin// las kyi sems dpa' nga gnas pas// ye shes ral gris 'debs shing spro// e ma'o las kyi
27b2(zha): che mchog gis// nyid kyi mtshan du gsol ba ni// cis kyang mi shigs mi phyed la// cis kyang ma g.yos ma 'dres pas// bde chen mchog tu gyur pas na// kun kyang /

28b1(zha): rgyal mo yis// phye zhing bshig dang bcom la sogs// dkrugs shing thal brdul phran bzhin// btsan zhing 'bar ba'i 'phro 'du 'dis// thams cad dril bu nyid pas na/

32a7(zha): bsod nams brten pa yin// ngo mtshar cho 'phrul rmad kyi chos// gzhan nas yod 'ongs ma yin te// thabs la brten pa'i shes rab nyid// de lta bu yi ngang du 'byung //
32b1(zha): shes rab dbyings kyi de bzhin nyid// thabs kyi phyag rgyar gyur pa'i phyir// ye shes la ni ye shes rol// ye shes rol pa nyid kyang gsog/ rgyal ba sngon byung skyob
32b2(zha): pa dang // byi ni rlabs ston pa 'ang de bzhin te// bya byed nus pa'i gzi byin gyis// sgyu ma rdo rje brtson po mchog/ cho ga lnga ni rdzogs byas shing // yo byad lnga ni rdzogs par
32b3(zha): ldan/ sngags kyi yan lag lnga rdzogs pas// ma nyams 'jug la rab brtson na// zhag ni sum cu phrag drug gram// bcu gnyis bcu bzhi bcu drug gis// dbang
32b4(zha): bskur rigs kyis dam pa'ang 'grub// de tshe bcu drug tshun chad kyis// sku lnga lhun gyis rdzogs pa ni// ye shes thig le de nyid la// ye shes thig le nyid snang ba//

33a3(zha): shes te/ gnyer na nye bar mnyam pa yi// ya mtshan chen po 'byung bar nges// dad med nyams na phung bar 'gyur// zhes ched du brjod do// gsang ba'i snying po
33a4(zha): de kho na nyid nges pa las// rdo rje bkod pa gsang ba dam tshig gi le'u ste bcu dgu pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rgyud kyi rgyal po sgyu 'phrul dra

33b1(zha): pa yis/ rang gi sa ba sgribs shing ba dag tu bcings// kun gyis yang dag rtog bya'i phyir// de bzhin chos sku'i gzugs brnyan yin// rtog dang mi rtog rang rig dang // /

33b5(zha): dkyil 'khor du// rang rig ye shes 'du 'phro yis// thams cad chos sku phyag rgya che// yang dag rtog pa'i khyad par gyis// ting 'dzin don rnams gsal bsgoms
33b6(zha): nas/ mA ma ka ni rgyun chags la// yang dag chos sku phyag rgya che// de bzhon ting 'dzin gsal bsgoms nas// don mchog ma lus rdzogs pa'i phyir// mkha' la

40a2(zha): dang bdud rtsi 'grub// A li kA li phyag rgya yis// sku gsung thugs kyi mchog ldan pa// thams cad thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// shas 'jug mtshan nyid 'byor

40a4(zha): dag 'dzin med kyi// khyad par sa la gnas 'gyur yin// pha rol phyin pa kun tu rdzogs// thabs dang shes rab thabs kyi mchog/ shes rab mchog gi mchog gyur pa'i/
40a5(zha): sa yi khyad par bcu dang gsum// rgyu 'bras khyad par lhun gyis rdzogs// mkha' dkyil dang ba'i dbyings nyi zla// ye shes rgyal po stangs dbyal bsgom// rgyal ba'i
40a6(zha): dkyil 'khor thams cad kun// ma lus par ni bsgom par 'gyur// dus bzhi phyogs bcu gang nas kyang // rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnyed mi 'gyur// sems nyid rdzogs pa'i//
40a7(zha): sangs rgyas te// sangs rgyas gzhan du mtshol cig/ dkyil 'khor kun tu rab sbyor bas// dkyil 'khor thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// cho ga lhag gam mtshanga'ang //
40b1(zha): skyon nyid dag ste nyes pa med// ces brjod pas/ rol mo'i sprin gyis mnyes par gyur to// sku gsung thugs yon tan 'phrin las rdo rje las/ rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig 'di phyung ngo //
40b2(zha): a ho/ ma mthong dngos la chags pa yis// chos rnams ming du btags pa tsam// 'gro drug dus gnas ming cho gas khyad par rab snang ba'i// zab chen spyod yul log por
40b3(zha): rtogs rtags ming tsam pa// a li kA li la sogs 'dod pa'i snying po de nyid de// phyag rgya glu tshig sku gsung thugs// thugs kyi thugs chen yon tan rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
40b4(zha): ni/ nyid de mnyam pa'i thugs su rab tugs la// mnyam nyid khyab pa'i stangs dbul yon tan mchog ste sngags kyi 'dzin las rdzogs// rdo rjegs ba'i tshig tu'o//
40b5(zha): gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ tshogs bsgrub pa'i le'u ste nyi shu bzhi pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa phyogs bcu dus bzhi
40b6(zha): sku gsung thugs rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor thams cad gcig tu 'dus nas// dgyes pa chen pos chos thams cad ye nas rdzogs pa chen por yenas lhun gyis rdzogs pa'i dam tshig
40b7(zha): shin tu gsang ba'i snying po'i sprin bkod pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// ma rtog pa dang log par rtogs// phyogs rtog yang dag
41a1(zha): nyid ma rtogs// 'dul ba dgongs pa gsang ba dang // rang bzhin gsang ba'i don rnams ni// yi ge sgra btags ming tshogs la// brten pa'i
41a2(zha): tshig gis rab mtshon te// khong na ga ba sbas don 'byin pa// ston pa rdo rje'i thugs la gnas// dkyil 'khor ldan pa'i dkyil 'khor gyis// dkyil 'khor la ni dkyil
41a3(zha): 'khor bsgom// dkyil 'khor dkyil 'khor las 'byung ba// thugs kyi dkyil 'khor dkyil 'khor mchog/ gsang ba'i thig le dkyil 'khor dbyings// sku
41a4(zha): gsung thugs rig kun mnga' ba'i// bde gshegs kun gyi snying po rdzogs// 'byung ba shes rab rigs kyi yum// chen po rigs kyi de bzhin te// byang chub sems ni
41a5(zha): rdo rje'i tshogs// dbang po yul dus rigs pa rnams// kun tu bzang po'i dkyil 'khor la// bdag nyid chen po rtag pa yi// thugs kyi ye shes lngas blta zhing //
41a6(zha): snying po thig le ma nyam sbyor bas// bde ba'i ye shes rol mo yis// ye shes dgyes la mnyes pa 'bul// zag pa med pa'i bsod nams kyis// ye shes sgyu mar
41a7(zha): rang snang ba// rol mo'i dkyil 'khor mtha' yas mchog/ gsang ba'i thig le nyid kyi dbyings// de ni sangs rgyas kun gyi dngos// phyogs bcu dus bzhi
41b1(zha): mngon rdzogs pa'i// sku gsung yon tan 'phrin las thugs// ma lus bdag nyid zhal mthong ba// dbang sgyur mchog nyid dam pa yin// dkyil 'khor la
41b2(zha): gnas dkyil 'khor nyid// rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor lhun gyis grub// rgyan du dkyil 'khor ma lus thogs// rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor ma nyam sbyor las//
41b3(zha): thugs rjes dkyil 'khor yongs kyis 'byung // phyogs dus dkyil 'khor 'dul ba'i mgon// sgyu ma'i dkyil 'khor sgrol ba yis// bya byed med par dkyil 'khor spod//
41b4(zha): ye shes rdzogs pa'i dkyil 'khor la// thos bsam bsgom pa'i mnyam sbyor gyis// rang byung kun dam lhun gyis grub// 'di ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyis// bdo'
41b5(zha): ba ra mi mdzad dam tshig mchog/ gang zhig 'di la mos gyur pa// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor thams cad kyis// phyogs dus kun nas thams cad du// dkyil 'khor ma
41b6(zha): lus brtan pa yis// nye ba'i sras su dgongs par 'gyur// bskal pa zhing gi rdul snyed du// shin tu sbyangs la rab gnas shing // dkyil 'khor ma lus bsnyen pa yi//
41b7(zha): 'bras bu gsang chen 'di yin te// 'jig rten drug gi phyogs bcun// 'das dang da ltar byung ba yis// rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor ma lus pa// brnyes nas sku lnga lhun
42a1(zha): gyis rdzogs// 'byung dang ma 'ongs thams cad kun// 'di yis lhun gyis grub par 'gyur// 'di ni gsang chen nges pa yi// 'bras bu lam du
42a2(zha): gyur pa yin// rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor ma lus la// 'di las gsang ba'i nges don med// btsal kyang rgya la bas mi brnyes so// kun gyi phyag rgya chen po'i mchog/ thos
42a3(zha): bsam bsgom la rab sbyangs pa'i// shes rab mig ldan rnams kyis zung // snod ldan dang tshul bzang la rten// lus dang longs spyod gtong la sbyin// gzhan du na ma yang
42a4(zha): sbyin mi bya// rmongs la 'phyar bas gal te sbyin// dus min par ni srog zad nas// sreg dang sgrubs par yun rings gnas// zhes de bzhin gshegs pa nyid de bzhin
42a5(zha): goshegs pa nyid la ched du brjod do// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ shin tu gsang ba'i snying po man ngag gi le'u ste nyi shu lnga pa'o//
42a6(zha): nas bcom ldan 'das dpal kun tu bzang pos dgyes pa chen po'i ngang las// gsang ba 'byung ba zhes bya ba tshad du brjod pa'ide brjod do// e ma'o// thams cad ma lus
42a7(zha): dus gsum bde gshegs mchog/ gdod nas ma skyes rnam dag byang chub sems// rang bzhin dbyer med ga dang mtha' mi 'byed cing // ye nas mnyam pas rgyal brgya mtsho
42b1(zha): yin// 'gro 'ong med par dus gsum cig char rdzogs// dbye gsal med phyir bzang ngan blang dor med// rnam rtog nyid na ye shes rang bzhin te// rnam rtog mi skye ye
42b2(zha): shes brjod du med// bdag tu med pa'i skye mchog sngon sbyangs pa// khril 'ga' tsam gal te 'byung 'gyur zhing // snga rabs phyi sa 'byung dag dang dbyer med pa'i// mngon/
42b3(zha): sum sangs rgyas skye mchog de dag la// bskal pa 'ga' nas shes rab blo sbyangs pa// dad ldan 'ga' yi sa 'tsham par ci theg gis// bdag nyid ma mthong shes rgyud ma 'byor
42b4(zha): pa// gzhan du tshol zhing rmongs pa'i sems can gyis// bstan kyang ma thos mtshon kyang ma mthong ba// bdag dang gzhan du tshol bas sangs mi rgyas// de dang ma bral ston pa mi
42b5(zha): mthong zhing // bgrod par 'dod pas phyin par mi nus te// shes rgyud ci yin gang gis ngo shes shing // bya byed las 'phags kyi na da 'dug byed pa// gang zhig blo la spyod
42b6(zha): pa byang chub thob// ma spangs mtshan ma kun bral yong med pas// dran byed mi spang 'khor rgyun mi 'byed de// mi gnyis mi 'byed mngon sum sangs rgyas la// blo yi rig/
42b7(zha): pas spyod cing nan tan dang // mtshon cing brten pas byang chub thob mngon te// nam mkhar bzung bas sprin gyis khebs par 'gyur// nam mkha' med par gang gis shes pa
43a1(zha): / sbyin zhig 'byung zhing khebs par myi srid do// nus par dag pa'i gsung rlung sangs rgyas sa// thams cad yen sa mnyam par nam dag cig/
43a2(zha): mi rtogs ler gnas la rtog pa mdzad// bsnyad du med pas sna tshogs 'byung ba yin// bdag med bdag chen thams cad 'byung ba'i gter// ma bkag pa las rgyu zhing
43a3(zha): 'byung med pa'i// thams cad sems kyi ngang ste sems zhes gdags su med// ma bcos lhun gnas ye nas byang chub cing // thob rgyu med pas ye nas pa de gshegs yin// /
43a4(zha): zhes brjod pas/ chos dang sems kyi khams thams cad// rang bzhin sangs rgyas par de bzhin gshegs pa nyid kyis mkhyen to// mkhyen nas ji bzhin pa'i bdag nyid
43a5(zha): chen po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje sgyu 'phrul dra ba las rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig 'di phyung ngo // e ma'o ma bsgrubs grub chen
43a6(zha): po/ grub pa chen po ye shes che// blang dor med pa'i sa chen po// mi g.yo 'du 'bral med pa'i gzugs// rtog pa'i ye shes yid bzhin gtor// thams /
43a7(zha): cad la yang me long bzhin// bltas kyang gzugs brnyan mi snang ngo // gang na gsang chen 'di yod par// me mar mur gyi dong 'bog sa la// spu gri so ni gtams
43b1(zha): pa la/ 'dzegs nas bu dag 'gro bar byos// khong na gnas pa'i yang khong du// lcags kyi sgrom bu kha bsdam mo// dbyings nyid la ni nyid spyod phyir// dbyings
43b2(zha): nyid mchog gi gnas la spyod// de nyid mi gnas mya ngan 'das// zhes rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig tu'o// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ gsang ba chen po man ngag gtan
43b3(zha): la phab pa'i le'u ste nyi shu drug pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgyes pa chen pos mnyam pa'i dkyil 'khor la bzhugs nas/ nyid kyi skul
43b4(zha): thams cad ma lus par 'dus par bstan te// ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// 'das dang da ltar ma 'ongs dang // 'byung bar ma nges dus 'di dag/ snga phyi med par mnyam
43b5(zha): yin te// nges pa med par yang dag gsungs// 'jig rten 'das dang 'jig rten pa'i// rang dang phyi ru bstan pa dang // ji snyed brtan g.yo la sogs pa// sgyu ma mig yor
43b6(zha): tshul yin te// skyes bu blo rtsa la rab ldan pas// de la rtag tu mnyam sbyor zhing // sems can kun gyi zhing gyur par// de dang gnyis med dbyings su sbyor// thams cad
43b7(zha): thabs kyi mtshan nyid de// thabs la thabs ni rnam par sbyor// thabs chen thabs las phyung ba yi// de ni byang chub rdo rje'i mchog/ ji snyed brjod pa'i kha sgyur kyang // yang
44a1(zha): dag don gyi snying po ni// gang nas btsal kyang mi rnyed de// rang rig sgrib med dag pa yin// de la rtag 'grus goms pa ni// bsnyen pa'i dam pa de yin
44a2(zha): te/ de ni ma nor lam yin par// a yis bo d+hi rab tu bsdus// de bzhin nyid kyi dbyings nyid ni// gcig dang 'di zhes brjod du med// gnyis med dbyings kyi ngang du med// gsum
44a3(zha): du sna tshogs 'byung zhing 'phro// byin rlabs bsam yas mtha' yas mchog/ don bsdus gsung rab bzhi bcu gnyis// de las lhag pa'i don smra ba// de ni rnam dag lam min te//
44a4(zha): rang blos bsam pas 'phrul pa yin// thams cad rang rig byang chub sems// don lung gi tshad mar bshad// tshad bzhi phab pa'i don yin te// dgra pa rnam gsum tshul gnas
44a5(zha): shing // 'bru lnga 'dus pa'i thabs chen po// 'gro ba kun la rang bzhin gnas// bya ba byed la byas pa med// zad pa'i dus med yid bzhin gter// bum pa bzang dang yid
44a6(zha): bzhin mdzod// za ma tog dang rin chen rgyal// gzhan na yod 'ongs ma yin te// rang sems bsod nams brtan po yin// lha srin la sogs yod pa yi// nor 'dra rin chen
44a7(zha): ma yin te// bo d+hi dkor ni rin po che// bsam gyis mi khyab ji snyed pa// 'gro dang mi 'gro'i 'jig rten kun// sku dang gsung thugs mi zad ldan// rgyan gyis 'khor lo bsam
44b1(zha): mi khyab// dngos grub mchog gi snying po ni// dang po don rtogs mtha' mi gtong // chu srin phyag rgya ji bzhin du// spyod yul kun tu tshad dpag med// ces gsungs so//
44b2(zha): gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las/ phyogs bcu dus bzhi snod bcud pa dag la 'dus pa dang // longs spyod dang sku gsung thugs mi zad pa rgyan gyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i le'u
44b3(zha): ste nyi shu bdun pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis dkyil 'khor la// dgyes pa chen pos glu 'di blangs so// o/ phyogs
44b4(zha): bcu dus bzhi rdzogs pa yis// ye shes dkyil 'khor thig le che// bsod nams dkyil 'khor sku yi tshogs// snang stong thig le kun tu rdzogs ho// oM/ rdo rje bsod
44b5(zha): nam sa thig le cha// rdo rje ye shes dkyil 'khor ldan// rdo rje sgra chen mtha' yas pa// rdo rje rgyal po thig le rgyu ho// oM/ sku gsung thugs ni rdzogs pa che// yon
44b6(zha): ta na ba phrin las kun tu rdzogs// ye nas lhun rdzogs kun tu bzang // 'dus pa'i rdzogs chen thig le che ho// oM/ mi dmigs sgyu 'phrul mnyam pa'i dbyings// mtha' yas
44b7(zha): kun nas sna tshogs 'phro// mtha' yas kun nas lhun gyis thim// sna tshogs sku gsung thugs chen po ho// oM// phyogs bcu 'jig rten rdul snyed du// rgyal ba'i don rnams rdul
45a1(zha): phran snyed// sprul pa ba sa ma yas rdul phran gyis// skad cig yud la lhun gyis grub ho// o/ thams cad ma lu sa sku gsung thugs// sku
45a2(zha): gsung thugs kyi bdag nyid che// sku gsung thugs kyis kun tu khyab// sku gsung thugs kyi thig le che ho// zhes ched du bsgrags so// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa lnga//
45a3(zha): mnyes pa'i le'u ste nyi shu brgyad pa'o// / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs rdo rje'i bdag po/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi ngo bo nyid
45a4(zha): kyis/ khro bo'i dkyil 'khor du mngon par 'du bar mdzad do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bdag tu rmongs pa'i rtog pa dang / rtag pa la mngon par zhen pa dang / yang dag pa'i lam dang
45a5(zha): bral ba dag/ gab pa'i gsang ba ma rtog par/ sbas pa'i gsang ba la mngon par 'chel nas/ rgyu dang 'bras bu la rmongs pas/ srid pa'i sa bon rtsub mos 'phangs nas/ mtshams
45a6(zha): med pa'i rab tu tsha ba'i dmyal bar skyes so// de rab tu tsha ba'i sdug bsngal drag pos gdungs pa dang / 'dod pas gdungs nas/ 'di bas shin tu grang yang ci ma rung mnyam pa'i mo la/
45a7(zha): rab tu sbrebs pa dang / pad+ma ltar gas pa'i sdug bsngal drag po dag gis rab tu nyen pa/ de lta bu'i sdug bsngal tsha ba la sogs pa brgyad dang / grang ba la sogs pa brgyad po dag tu 'jig rten
45b1(zha): gyi kham sa brgyud cing / bskal pa chen po stong phrag bcu gnyis su myong ngo // de nas rnam par smin pa de zad pa dang / yi dgas ltogs pa dang skom pa'i sdug bsngal gyis nyen pa dang / 'dod
45b2(zha): pa'i dngos po rnams yid du mi 'ong ba dang / gdug cing rtsub pa'i dngos po sna tshogs su gyur pa dang / yong med par yang gyur cing shin tu rid cing skams pa dang / lus dang yan
45b3(zha): lag dang / dbang po mi'i tsham par gyur pa/ bskal pa chen po drug tu skyes so// de nas las kyi sgrib pa rtsub mo'i rnam par smin pa de khad kyis bsrabs pa dang / sngon gyi srid pas mtshams
45b4(zha): sbyar nas/ yi dgas srin po chen po rab tu gdug pa dang gtum po/ lus gcig la mgo brgya pa dang / mgo sna tshogs pa dang / lus brgyal mgo gcig pa dang / lu sa sna tshogs pa
45b5(zha): dang / yan lag mang po dang / yan lag sna tshogs pa dang / gdug pa'i lag cha sna tshogs thogs pa/ 'khor rab tu gtum po mang po dang / 'jigs pa'i gzugs sna tshogs pa dang /
45b6(zha): 'jigs pa'i nga ro sgra skad sna tshogs par sgrogs pa dang / gzugs dang / nga bo dang / dri dang / kha rA ngas kyis thams cad spyi bung zhes byed pa dang / rab tu 'jigs pa'i rlung nag dang //
45b7(zha): grang ba dang / tsha ba'i dbugs kyi sa phyogs bcu kun tu khams 'khrug par byed pa/ nad bzhi brgya rtsa bzhis 'debs par byed pa/ myos shing nyams par byed pa'i mthus klu'i ris
46a1(zha): dang / lha ma yin gyi ris dang / lha'i ris dang / tshangs pa'i ris dang / 'od gsal dang / dge rgyas dang / 'bras bu che ba'i lha man chad dbang du bsdus
46a2(zha): so// de sngon gyis brten pa'i stobs thams cad mkhyen pas gzigs nas/ thugs rjes 'dul bar gyur te/ thams cad kyis mtshan nyid bstan pa'i glu 'di blangs so// e ma'o//
46a3(zha): 'gro ba yongs ni bde gshegs la ma yin te// sdug bsngal sreg mdzad sgyu ma'i sprul par snang // yon tan rmad 'byung che ba'i rang bzhin 'di// sdug bsngal kun la bshes gnyen mgon/
46a4(zha): ba yin// rmongs dang 'khrul pa rab sel zhe sdang 'joms// kun 'byung bde ba rdo rje sku mchog ste// rdzogs ldan mdzad pa'i 'phrin las bsam yas pas// thugs rje chen po'i
46a5(zha): dbang gi sa bdud rnams 'joms// sku mdog sna tshogs thabs mkhas bsam yas la// rol pa'i rtse mor 'gro ba'i don mdzad cing // byang chub sems kyi lam la gnas par mdzad// /
46a6(zha): 'gro ba kun las bde ba gcig pu pa// a ho/ dgyes pa'i mnyes pa nyid la gnas par mdzad// byin brlabs kun gyis bde ba nyid la snang // zhes brjod pa sa/ de bzhin gshegs
46a7(zha): pa nyid de bzhin gshegs pa nyid la/ kun nas rnam par rgyal ba nyid du mkhyen nas mnyes par gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i che ba'i rdo rje bkod pa'i sgyu
46b1(zha): 'phrul dra ba las/ 'jig rten drug gi phyogs bcu'i srid pa gsum gyi bdag po 'dul zhing rgyal chen po gzi brjid chen po ston pa'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang /
46b2(zha): gsung dang / thugs rdo rje'i bdag po/ bcom ldan 'das dgyes pa chen po khro bo'i rgyal po sprin chen po rnam par 'phro ba'i sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te//
46b3(zha): de bzhin nyid kyi dbyings nyid las khro mo dbang phyug chen mo mngon du phyung ste/ hi hi zhes dgyes pa'i gzi mdangs kyis rin chen pad+ma rgyas par mdzad nas/ gnyis su med pa'i 'khril
46b4(zha): ba'i dgyes pas thim nas/ byang chub kyi sems kyis sprin chen las/ hUM hUM hUM bi shwa badz+ra kro d+ha dz+wA la dz+wa la maN+Da la/ phaT phaT phaT ha la ha la ha la hUM/ zhes brjod pas/ 'jig
46b5(zha): rten drug gi phyogs bcu mtha' yas par khyab par khro bo'i dkyil 'khor gyi tshogs stong gsum gyi 'jig rten tsam/ phyogs bcur rdul phra mo snyed 'thon par gyur nas/ 'jig rten
46b6(zha): drug gi phyogs bcu thams cad g.yos/ rab tu g.yos/ kun tu g.yos so// 'ur bu ra/ rab tu'u ra'ur/ kun tu'u ra'ur ro// che mchem/ rab tu che mchem/ kun tu chen

47a1(zha): thams cad na gnas pa'i dbang che ba dang / gzi brjid che ba dang / dpa' mthu che ba'i dbang phyug chen po la sogs pa thams cad brgyal/ rab tu brgyal
47a2(zha): kun tu brgyal bar gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das dgyes pa chen po nyid/ 'jigs byed chen po shin tu rngam pa skye bung zhes byed pa'i 'bar ba chen po'i khrag 'thung sku
47a3(zha): smug nag 'jigs ji ltar yang 'gyur ba/ dbu dang / phyag dang / zhabs stong khams kyi rdul snyed mtshon cha tshogs 'dzin pa de/ dbu gsum phyag dru ga zhabs bzhir gyur te/ dur khrod
47a4(zha): chen por dgyes nas/ khrag gi rgya mtsho 'khrugs pa'i dkyil na/ ke ra rus chen po ri rab kyi steng gi 'bar ba chen po glog gi 'khor lo'i dkyil na/ dbang phyug chen po dang / dur khrod kyi
47a5(zha): bdag po drags pa chen po khyo shug gi gdan la/ brkyang bskum gyi tshul du bzhugs so// khro bo'i dkyil 'khor gyi sprin phung gi tshogs de dag kyang / la la ni dpal khrag 'thung chen po rdo rjer
47a6(zha): gyur te/ shar phyogs su bzhugs so// la la ni dpal khrag 'thung chen po rin po cher gyur te/ lho phyogs su bzhugs so// la la ni dpal khrag 'thung chen po pad+mar gyur te//
47a7(zha): nub phyogs su bzhugs so// la la ni dpal khrag 'thung chen po kun tu las su gyur te/ byang phyogs su bzhugs so// de dag kun kyang 'jigs byed chen po'i cha lugs dang /

63a1(zha): gcig tu gyur nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa nyid de bzhin gshegs pa nyid la ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// byed pa rdo rje mchog nyid kyis// sgyu 'phrul lam

69b1(zha): gang la bya ba'i gzugs bzung nas// kha dog dmar po'i tshon phye yis// de yi snying nang ba dag zhugs la// oM zhes bya ba'i sngags bzlas nas// rgyal mo zhang blon dbang chen dang //

70a1(zha): yis// mi snang ba yi gzugs su 'char// bdag gi lus la chud par 'gyur// gling ngam dur khrod gnas rnams su// nga yi 'dod pa chos dbang gis//

177a7(zha): pa'i dkyil 'khor nyid// rdo rje chen po thugs kyi mchog/ rigs bdag rgyal po'i ngo bo nyid// bde gshegs 'khor lo lta bu'i dbyig/ zhing khams mtha' yos
177b1(zha): rgyal ba'i tshogs// yon tan rin chen che gnas 'byor// de dag gdod nas kun rdzogs mdzad// gsung gi pad+ma rnam par dag/ chos kyi rgyun gyi ting 'dzin gyi//
177b2(zha): 'phrin las kun mthar phyin pas// rigs kyi dkyil 'khor kun rdzogs mdzad// chos dbyings me long mnyam pa nyid// so sor kun rtog/ bya ba zug/ nyon mongs lam kun
177b3(zha): rnam dag pa'i// rigs kyi bde gshegs thams cad mkhyen// byang chub sems nyid 'gyur ba med// ma 'dres las kun rnam par dag/ yon tan tshogs kun lhun grub cing //
177b4(zha): chags pa chen pos kun spyod pa// de dag 'phrin las sna tshogs kyis// rang rigs zhing khams chen por sbyor// phyogs bcu kun nas 'khril ba yi// 'byung ba che nas rnam
177b5(zha): pa rA dag/ gsal snang rdo rje dbang phyug dbyings// sra mkhregs bde gshegs phyag rgya ste// sdud cing gzung med yon tan dbyings// gsal dro smin pa pad+ma'i chos// bskyod
177b6(zha): pa'i 'phrin las kun rdzogs pa'i// don 'thun rtags kyi phyag rgya nyid// btsun mo dam pa'i cha lugs kyis// de dag dkyil 'khor bstan par mdzad// dam pa kun dang
177b7(zha): tshogs pa'i// tshul rnams yang dag rdzogs pa'i skus// khams gsum phye nas rnam dag cing // zag med rigs kyi dkyil 'khor nyid// til gyi gang bu ji lta bar//
178a1(zha): bar mtshams med par mtha' yas pa'o// de tshe 'khor gyi byang chub sems// dkyil 'khor chen po'i phyogs kun nas// rdo rje bkod pa'i gar
178a2(zha): dang ni/ glur bcas mngon par 'khod gyur pa// rgyu dang 'bras bu'i bdag nyid can// smon lam thig le'i stobs rdzogs pa'i// dkyil 'khor chen po 'ganas mdzes
178a3(zha): par/ ye shes 'gro ga nas rnam par dag/ byang chub sems nyid sa chen po// kun bya ba rdul phran namakha' nyid// thugs rjes pad+ma sna tshogs ston// las kyi 'phrin
178a4(zha): las stobs rdzogs non// rnam shes bzhi yi bdag nyid kyi// de dag yul bcas dag par mdzad// thabs bcas ma 'dres byams pa'i stobs// sgrib med mun pa'i
178a5(zha): cho gas sel zhing // kun nas spyod pa bzang po nyid// shes rab chen po'i chos mthar phyin// gsung gi dbang po rnam dag pas// rigs kyi ye shes gsal bar sbyor//
178a6(zha): ma lus gzugs sgra dri ro'i tshi gas// lha mo'i dkyil 'khor rnam par dag/ de dag thabs dang shes rab kyis// yi ge'i gnas kun mnyam pa nyid// kun na so kun tu
178a7(zha): ba sa ma byas pa'i// dus rnams lha mo'i bdag nyid du// mi mthun mtshan ma'i phyogs 'joms byed// der rdzogs gnyen po'i stobs dang ldan// phyogs kyi don
178b1(zha): rnams 'jo mas mdzad cing // 'phrin las rigs kyi ye shes rdzogs// las kyi chos kun rnam dag pa'i// khro bo chen po mthu stobs ldan// rtag chad mtshan ma'i g.yul rnams
178b2(zha): 'joms// tshad med bzhi rdzogs rtogs nas sel// lcags kyu zhags pa lcags sgrog dril// phyi nang dkyil 'khor bstan mdzad cing // rigs kyi 'khor lo kun
178b3(zha): rdzogs dag/ stong kha ma sa kun tu mtha' yas pa ra// de dag dkyil 'khor gsal bar snang // gnyis med mnyam pa chen po'i sku// grangs med brjod kyi sa mi yang
178b4(zha): ba/ gnyis su med par brtan par bzhugs pa'o// de nas rigs kyi sangs rgyas kun// rang gi dkyil 'khor ji lta ba// mi gnyis don kun bstan
178b5(zha): mdzad de// ma 'dres stobs kyis rnam par dag/ de tshe bde gshegs mthu stobs kyis// sku gsum byin rlab sa ba sa ma yas dang // dkyil 'khor bkod pa kun snang
178b6(zha): mdzad/ sku gsung thugs kyi rnam 'phrul gyi// rol pa'i byin rlabs mtha' yas ston// mthar thug med pa'i 'jig rten 'dir// ngo mtshar mtha' ya sa lhas kyis
178b7(zha): gang / g.yo dang g.yo ba chen po dang // bskyod dang bskyod pa chen po yi// sgrub phrul rol pas ma lus kun// rnam dag dkyil 'khor gsal rdzogs mdzad// rigs
179a1(zha): kyi rgyal ba thams cad dang // byang chub sems rnams yi rangs te// sna tshogs mchod pas spro mdzad cing // yang dag don rdzogs gsol ba 'debs//
179a2(zha): sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rgyud chen po// sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba'i gnas// de dag mngon 'byung rdzogs byed pa'i// rgyu dang 'bras bu mtshungs pa'i don// rab tu mos pa smin//
179a3(zha): byed tsong // thabs kyi phyag rgya gsang ba nyid// stong phrag brgya pa'i rgyud chen po// mgon po rtswa ldan mtshungs pa'i lam// ma lus yul kun thabs 'di nyid// phag rgya'i
179a4(zha): dkyil 'khor bla na med// khyod nyid rgyal ba kun gyi yab// dang po rdo rje chen po nyid// rab tu mi gnas stobs rdzogs pa'i// bdag po chos kyi ting nge 'dzin// phrag rgyas
179a5(zha): zag me da kun grol ba'i// ye shes brtan pa'i gnas 'di nyid// mtshan ldan mtshan rnams kun nas rdzogs// a ma'o byang chub sems nyid don// de na sa yul kun
179a6(zha): rdzogs pa'i don// thugs rje ya she sa dr-i ma med// thams cad thabs la sa 'byung ba yi// byang chub sems 'di rang byang gnas// mi shig dkyil 'khor ba rtan pa nyid /
179a7(zha): bdag po rang gi stabs rdzogs pas// ye nas yul kun rnam par dag/ thugs rje chen pos snang ba'i shugs// byin rlabs yul bcas ji ltar snang // de dag rang gi las
179b1(zha): bzhin du// blo bur 'khrul pas rtog 'dzin cing // phyi nang yul sogs rnam dpyod pa// thugs rje dag pas ji ltar sgra la// de dag dkyil 'khor kun rdzogs pa'i// rigs
179b2(zha): kyi gnas rnams sbyor mdzad cing // phyag rgya gsang sngags stobs rdzogs pas// tshad med yul kun rdzogs pa nyid// dkyil 'khor chen po rnam grangs kyi// bye brag mkhas pa'i
179b3(zha): spyod yul las// rang bzhin lhun gyis grub pa dag/ don dam kun rdzob rnam par spod// sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang ba 'di// tshul bzhin dmigs par bya ba'i thabs// de las
179b4(zha): lhog pa'i don snang zhing // phyi rol 'byung tshogs 'gro bar bcas// sangs rgyas kun gyi rang bzhin te// dkyil 'khor rdzogs pa'i rigs mchog nyid// shes rab chen po
179b5(zha): yul mthar phyin// cha shas cha sha sa med pa yis// byang chub sems gnas drug pa'i gzungs// ma lus yul kun spong mdzad cing // gnyis med ye shes chen po'i bdag/
179b6(zha): chos kyi gnas kun rdzogs longs spyod// sprul pa'i sku rdzogs 'gro ba'i mgon// dkyil 'khor byin rlabs 'gro ba'i mgon// sgyu 'phrul bsgrub pa'i dkyil 'khor dang // lhag
179b7(zha): ba khro bo'i dkyil 'khor gyi// rang bzhin mngon par rdzogs pa'i shugs// ye shes dkyil 'khor ji lta bu// rang bzhin lhun gyis grub pa dang // rtog pas mngon par
180a1(zha): yus sbyor ba'i// thun mong khyad par rigs bcas rnams/ gdul bya kun gyi don bzhin du// bye brag ji ltar 'tshams par snang // 'dir ni lhag ma'i ting
180a2(zha): 'dzin dang // ting 'dzin dkyil 'khor ma bcos pa// de dag rgyu dang 'bras bu yi// tshul bzhin bstan pas rnam par spyod// 'gro ba 'dul ba'i ting 'dzin gyis// dkyil 'khor
180a3(zha): phyag rgya sngags rdzogs pa'i// khro bo'i dkyil 'khor mngon snang zhing // rang gi 'phrin las brtan pa'i bdag/ tshogs bsgrub ting 'dzin rgya chen po// bsod nams ye shes mngon
180a4(zha): rdzogs byed// 'phrin las bye brag stobs kyis ni// ting 'dzin dkyil 'khor dag spyod pa// bzhi brgyad mnyam pa chen po'i dbyings// de dgra 'phrin las ji lta bus//
180a5(zha): yang dag bya ba rdzogs par 'gyur// gzugs brnyan dkyil 'khor rgya chen pos// sa gzhi mnyam la ga nas rdzogs pa// phyogs mtshams kun tu shis pa'i las// mngon par
180a6(zha): bsngags pa ji lta bu// yang dag dkyil 'khor thig gdab cing // yang dag tshon gyi las rnams dang // phyag rgya'i bye brag kun rdzogs pa'i// rgyun cha sa bkod pa bla na med//
180a7(zha): dngos grub 'phrini la sa lha gnas shing // dkyil 'khor bsgrub pa'i tshul dag gis// las kyi lhag chad rdzogs byed cing // mnyes shing shis pas 'dod pa'i don//
180b1(zha): ye shes dkyil 'khor ji lta bar// dam tshig dkyil 'khor che nas sbyor// lha gnas sta gon bum pa dang // dkyil 'khor chen po'i gnas rnams rdzogs// de dag bkra
180b2(zha): shi sa cho ga bzang // nye bar bsnyen pa sa gsal bar 'gyur// 'jug pa'i cho ga tshul bzhin du// rnam gsum nus pa mthu dang ldan// bde gshegs byin rlabs rgyud pa'i
180b3(zha): lam// dad brtson shes rab ting 'dzin stobs// sbyin sreg gas dra ba'i las rdzogs shing // 'dod pa'i las kun nye bar sbyor// mchod sbyin rgya chen gtor ma'i tsho gas//
180b4(zha): de dag yul kun rnam dag 'gyur// sgyu 'phrul rgyas pa'i tshul gyis ni// lam lnga dang ni nyi shu rtsa lnga dang // sum cu rtso lnga lnga bcu rdzogs// bye brag dkyil 'khor
180b5(zha): 'gye ba ni// cho ga kun rdzogs mngon par bsngags// sangs rgyasra theg pa ba sam yas pa// de dag tshul rnams mtha' yas pa// sku gsung yon tan 'phrin las
180b6(zha): thugs/ ta ma lus kun 'dus rnam par dag/ thabs ldan rdzogs pa'i gang zag tu// smin pa'i lam mchog bla na med// byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed cing // rang
180b7(zha): ga dem bcas sdom pa rdzogs// yul mchog khyad par 'phags pa las// byin rlabs sngags kyi nor bu blangs// phan dang nus pa'i dbang thob cing // rang bzhin dam tshig
181a1(zha): brtan pa ra ga nas// de dag khyad par bye brag gi/ don kun gsang bas mngon gyur pa// thun mong sdom pa thams cad dang // gsang ba'i dam
181a2(zha): tshig bla na med// lnga gsum nyi shu rtsa lnga dang // sum brgya la sogs bye brag gis// thabs kyi theg pa rnam par da pags// de dag gsang ba chen po'i tshes// khyad
181a3(zha): par dam tshig rnam pa bzhis// thams cad gnyis med mnyam pa nyid// ma lus yul kun rnam dag cing // nges pa'i don rdzogs zab mo nyid// grog sra brtan mi mthun
181a4(zha): phyogs bcas pa'i// khyad par yul kun ji lta bus// rang rig gnas rnams bgrod par byed// thun mong la sogs rnam dpyad pa// ma lus brten cing 'brel pa'i chos// /
181a5(zha): thams cad tshul 'dis rtse gos byed cing // skad cig yud la lhun gyis grub// dgug dang btang dang bcing dang dgrol// go so dang bsad dang 'pha ma dang rgyal// gnas
181a6(zha): kyi phyag rgya kun rdzogs pas// don kun gsang ba ston par byed// bdud rtsir 'gyur zhing 'byung ba dang // bzhi brgya rtsa bzhi'i nad sel zhing // tshe dbang bkra shis byin
181a7(zha): rlabs stobs// ma lus kun 'dus rdzogs par 'gyur// thun mong rnam par bsngags po'i chos// thams cad las byung stobs ston pas// de dag gsang ba chen po'i
181b1(zha): mthus// ma lus rdzogs shing rnam par dag/ nam mkha' rdo rje sgra 'byung zhing // 'bar nas me yang 'tshig pa dang // chu rgyun 'bab pa'ang de bzhin te// 'jig rten
181b2(zha): khams ni 'thor ba dang // thams cad stong zhing lhung byed las// byin rlabs ngo mtshar yul 'byung bas// ga sang sngags phyag rgya'i ting 'dzin stobs// de dag tshul rnam/
181b3(zha): kun rdzogs pas// 'phags pa kun gyi gnas rdzogs pa'i// 'a phags pa kun gyi gan sa rdzogs te// rigs kyi zhing kham sa che ra ga na sa 'byor// sku dang yang shes sbrul

182b1(zha): 'bras bu'i tshul gyis bsgyur bcas sbyong // mtha' yas zhing khams chen po'i gnas// kun tu bzang po'i dkyil 'khor rnam par dag/ rdo rje sems dpa' sgyu 'phrul

183a1(zha): mtha' yas rdzogs// chos kyi sku la sa bzhengs mdzad de// thugs rje chen po'i rnam 'phrul gyis// snod bcud dkyil 'khor gsang ba'i bdag/ rigs

183a4(zha): 'das/ dus gsum kun gyi mi 'gyur zhing // de dag skad cig cir mi snang // de nas 'byung sogs rnam dag cing // skye 'gro tha dad de nyid dbyings// yod med mtha' bzhi las

184b1(zha): bzhin bde ba'i ngo bo las// mi gnyis nyams su myong ba'i tshul// e ma ho sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// rnam par thar pa chen po'i mchog/ ske 'gag gnas dang dmigs

192b3(zha): rang bzhin gnyis su rdzogs pa las// rnam par bkod pa ci zhig 'gru ba// bya ba med las bya ba'i tshul// bden pa gnyis su dbyer med pa// 'di dag sangs rgyus theg pa'i

192b5(zha): bu bzang po'i tshul// snying po don kun rdzogs pas na// ma lus kun 'dus gtan la 'bebs// ji snyed theg pa bsam yas pa// de dag gsang ba'i snying po bzhi//
192b6(zha): don kun ngo bo rnam dag pa'i// de nyid nges par rmad du 'byung // de ltar bstan pa sna tshogs pas// ma lus chos rnams yang dag rdzogs// rang bzhin ye shes dkyil 'khor

221a6(zha): kun gyi las dag par// de dag rdzas kun mngon par snang // rang bzhin ye shes kun rdzogs gnas// rigs kyi 'khor lo yum dang bcas// gnyis med rol pa'i byin rlabs kyis//
221a7(zha): 'byung ba'i tshogs rnams bshig pa dang // spro zhing sbar dang bkod mdzad de// snga ma'i gnas kun gzhan 'gyur ba/ bya ba chen po'i don ston mdzad// oM A hUM swA hA/ sa ma mo/
221b1(zha): ga ni rti swA hA/ oM man+ta la garbe hUM swA b+ha wa sa ma yA haM/ oM sarba shu d+ho stA/ oM ba ri garba sid+d+ha hUM/ oM gA ga na sam+b+ho ta na hUM/ de dag yul bcas 'gyur byed cing // rigs tshogs phyag
221b2(zha): rgya sngags dang bcas// ting 'dzin spros pa'i tshul nyid kyis// de nyid ga nas mchog 'grub par 'gyur// dpag tshad brgyad dang stong la sogs// rab tu grags pa'i mkha sa
221b3(zha): rnams kyis// tha snyad yul rnams sbyong mdzad cing // 'dod pa'i dngos grub kun gyi gzugs// rang sa mas dri med sbyang ba'i mthus// dpag bsam shing dang rin chen sogs//
221b4(zha): rdzas kyi mchog rnams 'grub byed cing // de nas longs spyod tshim par 'gyur// thun mong mngon par shes pa'i stobaso// thabs kyi bye brag mtha' yas pa// rigs pa bzang
221b5(zha): po'i phyag rgya yis// 'khor lo rnam bcas kun tu sbyor// ral gri mig sman bcud len dang // rkang mgyogs ga ser 'gyur bum pa bzang // mkha' 'gro 'jig rten kun spyod pa/
221b6(zha): 'khor lo sogs pa rigs pa'i bdag/ rdo rje a dza ru bu'i tshogs// ma g.yos kun tu khyab byed pa'i// dngos grub la sogs grangs med ba dag/ rang gi lha yi ting 'dzin rdzogs/
221b7(zha): dkyil 'khor kun nas dkyil 'khor ldan// 'khrul 'khor nyis rami sbyor ba dag/ sngags dang phyag rgya dbang sbyar te// bsam gtan yul tshogs kun gsal ba// rgyu 'bras
222a1(zha): bye brag tha dad rnams// rang gi rkyen gyis rnam par 'grub// pho brang dkyil 'khor bzang po nyid// rtse gcig ldan pas bstan par 'gyur// oM sar+b+ba a/
222a2(zha): nu ra ga sa mo ga ta na hU/ oM mahA sa ma yA hri ta ni man garba hUM// rA ga dz+wa la dz+wa la pra mo ta na hA// oM sarba ga ni log na pra te sha ra hUM phaT swA hA/ khams gsum thams cad rnam pa ra dag/
222a3(zha): rigs kyi dkyil 'khor kun rdzogs byed// yang dag bden pa'i byin rlabs kyis// 'di nas las kun 'grub gyur cig/ sangs rgyas kun gyi gzi brjid dang / gsang ba sngags
222a4(zha): kyi 'khor lo mchog/ phyag rgya bden pa'i byin rlabs kyis// las kun dngos grub stobs rdzogs shog/ smon lam rnam par dag pa yi// byin rlabs tshogs nyid rdzogs pa nyid//
222a5(zha): ji srid bdag gi dbang du ni// don kun bsam pa'i las rdzogs shog/ bsnyen pa'i yan lag rnam bzhi yis// rdo rje bkod pa mtha' yas mchog/ gtso bo rigs kyi sku rdzogs
222a6(zha): pas// phyag rgya'i yul kun bstan par mdzad// nye bar bsnyen pa'i yan lag bzhis// don chos lha mo gzungs kyi tshogs// sbyor ba'i phyag rgya kun spyod cing // sangs rgyas
222a7(zha): thams cad bstan pa'i bdag/ bsgrub pa'i yan lag rnam bzhi yis// zhing khams chen po kun sbyor zhing // phyi nang yul kun rdzogs pa nyid// dkyil 'khor bstan pa'i
222b1(zha): 'khor lo rdzogs// sgrub pa chen po'i yan lag bzhis// sangs rgyas thams cad sbyor mdzad cing // rten dang brten bcas rnam par 'phrul// phyogs dus ye shes rdzogs pa'i
222b2(zha): mchog/ rab dga'i tshul gyis mngon sum du// thabs kyi 'khor lo 'gog pa dang // shes rab 'khor lo 'gog pa'i mchog/ phyag rgya gsang ba'i sgrub pa nyid// gnyis med
222b3(zha): don gyis rnam par spyod// nye bar bstan pa'i rdzas rnams la// rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i mthus// rigs mchog phyag rgya gsal 'gyur zhing // 'khrul 'khor phyag rgya'i

222b5(zha): pa'i phyag rgya nyid// mtshan ma'i dngos grub sna tshogs pa// rang gi rten bzhin skye bar 'gyur// sku dang gsung thugs las byung ba'i// dngos grub snying po'i lha gnas mchog/
222b6(zha): rang gnas mthong ba'i ye shes kyis// sa gsum dbang phyug rdzogs par 'gyur// phyag rgya'i cho ga gang rdzogs pa// lam kun skyed pa'i yan lag ste// mi shig dkyil 'khor sngags
222b7(zha): kyi mthus// bya ba chen po'i don rdzogs shing // zag pa med pa'i dngos grub mchog/ rab tu bstan pas 'bras bu nyid// sangs rgyas kun gyi ye shes mchog/ dus gsum
223a1(zha): rdo rje 'dus ma byas// snang dang stong pa las grol zhing // mtha' dbus du sa sogs mtshan rnams grol// gnyis med ye shes dngos grub mchog/
223a2(zha): rang ga nas byang chub sems la bskyed// skye 'gag rtag chad spros pa'i gzhi// zhen pa'i tha snyad yul bral zhing // khyab dang khyab byed sna tshogs dag/ yang dag chos
